srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Admiral_Faddey_Faddeyevich_Bellingshausen.jpg/150px-Admiral_Faddey_Faddeyevich_Bellingshausen.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Admiral_Faddey_Faddeyevich_Bellingshausen.jpg/200px-Admiral_Faddey_Faddeyevich_Bellingshausen.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Fabian_Gottlieb_von_Bellingshausen" title="Fabian Gottlieb von Bellingshausen">Fabian Gottlieb von Bellingshausen</a></b>&#167;<br/>(1778&#8211;1852)<br/>Russian admiral, circumnavigator, cartographer\n</td>\n<td>Bellingshausen took part in the <a href="/wiki/First_Russian_circumnavigation" title="First Russian circumnavigation">first Russian circumnavigation</a> under <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ivan_Krusenstern" title="Ivan Krusenstern">Ivan Krusenstern</a> on <a href="/wiki/Nadezhda_(1802_Russian_ship)" title="Nadezhda (1802 Russian ship)"><i>Nadezhda</i></a> in 1803&#8211;06. He himself led another Russian circumnavigation in 1819&#8211;21 on the sloop <i><a href="/wiki/Vostok_(sloop-of-war)" title="Vostok (sloop-of-war)">Vostok</a></i>, together with <a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Lazarev" title="Mikhail Lazarev">Mikhail Lazarev</a> on <i><a href="/wiki/Mirny_(sloop-of-war)" title="Mirny (sloop-of-war)">Mirny</a></i> &#8211; this expedition was the first to discover the continent of <a href="/wiki/Antarctica" title="Antarctica">Antarctica</a> on January 28, 1820 (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Style" title="New Style">New Style</a>). They also discovered and named <a href="/wiki/Peter_I_Island" title="Peter I Island">Peter I Island</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zavodovski_Island" title="Zavodovski Island">Zavodovski</a>, <a href="/wiki/Leskov_Island" title="Leskov Island">Leskov</a> and <a href="/wiki/Visokoi_Island" title="Visokoi Island">Visokoi Islands</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Antarctic_peninsula" title="Antarctic peninsula">Antarctic peninsula</a> mainland and <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Island" title="Alexander Island">Alexander Island</a> (Alexander Coast), and made discoveries in the tropical waters of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pacific" title="Pacific">Pacific</a>, including <a href="/wiki/Vostok_Island" title="Vostok Island">Vostok Island</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bellingshausen_12-1"><a href="#cite_note-bellingshausen-12">[12]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Bellingshausen_Island" title="Bellingshausen Island">Bellingshausen Island</a> (Atlantic), <a href="/wiki/Bellingshausen_Sea" title="Bellingshausen Sea">Bellingshausen Sea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bellingshausen_Station" title="Bellingshausen Station">Bellingshausen Station</a>, <a href="/wiki/Motu_One_(Society_Islands)" title="Motu One (Society Islands)">Bellinshausen Island</a> (Pacific), <a href="/wiki/Faddey_Islands" title="Faddey Islands">Faddey Islands</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bellingshausen_Plate" title="Bellingshausen Plate">Bellingshausen Plate</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bellinsgauzen_crater" title="Bellinsgauzen crater">Bellinsgauzen crater</a> (Moon), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/3659_Bellingshausen" title="3659 Bellingshausen">3659 Bellingshausen</a> (minor planet).</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Platinum_coin5318-0006R.gif"><img alt="Antarctica" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="240" data-file-width="240" decoding="async" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Platinum_coin5318-0006R.gif/120px-Platinum_coin5318-0006R.gif" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Platinum_coin5318-0006R.gif/180px-Platinum_coin5318-0006R.gif 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/4/47/Platinum_coin5318-0006R.gif 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Platinum_coin5318-0006R.gif" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i><a href="/wiki/Vostok_(sloop-of-war)" title="Vostok (sloop-of-war)">Vostok</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Mirny_(sloop-of-war)" title="Mirny (sloop-of-war)">Mirny</a></i> in <a href="/wiki/Antarctica" title="Antarctica">Antarctica</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#ffffd0;">\n<th align="center" scope="row">\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Lev_Berg" title="Lev Berg">Lev Berg</a></b>!<br/>(1876&#8211;1950)<br/>geographer, biologist\n</td>\n<td>Berg studied and determined the depth of the lakes of <a href="/wiki/Central_Asia" title="Central Asia">Central Asia</a>, including <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Balkhash_Lake" title="Balkhash Lake">Balkhash Lake</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Issyk_Kul" title="Issyk Kul">Issyk Kul</a>. He researched the <a href="/wiki/Ichthyology" title="Ichthyology">ichthyology</a> of Central Asia and <a href="/wiki/European_Russia" title="European Russia">European Russia</a>. He developed <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dokuchaev" title="Dokuchaev">Dokuchaev</a>\'s doctrine of <a href="/wiki/Biome" title="Biome">biomes</a> and <a href="/wiki/Climatology" title="Climatology">climatology</a> and was one of the founders of the Geographical Institute, now the Faculty of Geography of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saint_Petersburg_University" title="Saint Petersburg University">Saint Petersburg University</a>. In 1940&#8211;50 Berg was the President of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Soviet_Geographical_Society" title="Soviet Geographical Society">Soviet Geographical Society</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:LakeBalkhash-EO.jpg"><img alt="Balkhash Lake" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="297" data-file-width="478" decoding="async" height="75" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/LakeBalkhash-EO.jpg/120px-LakeBalkhash-EO.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/LakeBalkhash-EO.jpg/180px-LakeBalkhash-EO.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/LakeBalkhash-EO.jpg/240px-LakeBalkhash-EO.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:LakeBalkhash-EO.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Balkhash_Lake" title="Balkhash Lake">Balkhash Lake</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#dfdfff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row">\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Vitus_Bering" title="Vitus Bering">Vitus Bering</a></b>^<br/>(1681&#8211;1741)<br/>Russian Navy captain-commander\n</td>\n<td>Returning from the <a href="/wiki/East_Indies" title="East Indies">East Indies</a>, Bering joined the Russian Navy in 1703. He became the main organiser of the <a href="/wiki/Great_Northern_Expedition" title="Great Northern Expedition">Great Northern Expedition</a> to explore northern Asia. In 1725, Bering went overland to <a href="/wiki/Okhotsk" title="Okhotsk">Okhotsk</a>, crossed to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kamchatka" title="Kamchatka">Kamchatka</a>, and aboard <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Gabriel" title="St. Gabriel">Sv. Gavriil</a></i> mapped some 3500&#160;km of the <a href="/wiki/Bering_Sea" title="Bering Sea">Bering Sea</a> coast and passed the <a href="/wiki/Bering_Strait" title="Bering Strait">Bering Strait</a> in 1728&#8211;29. Later, <a href="/wiki/Ivan_Fyodorov_(navigator)" title="Ivan Fyodorov (navigator)">Ivan Fyodorov</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Gvozdev" title="Mikhail Gvozdev">Mikhail Gvozdev</a> aboard the same <i>Sv. Gavriil</i> sighted the <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaskan</a> shore in 1732. Having organised a major <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Second_Kamchatka_expedition" title="Second Kamchatka expedition">Second Kamchatka expedition</a>, Bering and <a href="/wiki/Aleksei_Chirikov" title="Aleksei Chirikov">Aleksei Chirikov</a> sailed from <a href="/wiki/Okhotsk" title="Okhotsk">Okhotsk</a> in 1740 aboard <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Peter" title="St. Peter">Sv. Piotr</a></i> and <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Paul_of_Tarsus" title="Paul of Tarsus">Sv. Pavel</a></i>, founded <a href="/wiki/Petropavlovsk-Kamchatsky" title="Petropavlovsk-Kamchatsky">Petropavlovsk-Kamchatsky</a>, and headed together to <a href="/wiki/North_America" title="North America">North America</a> in 1741, until separated by storm. Bering discovered the southern coast of <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a>, landed near <a href="/wiki/Kayak_Island" title="Kayak Island">Kayak Island</a> and discovered the <a href="/wiki/Aleutian_Islands" title="Aleutian Islands">Aleutian Islands</a>. Chirikov discovered the shores of America near <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aleksander_Archipelago" title="Aleksander Archipelago">Aleksander Archipelago</a> and safely returned to Asia. Bering, however, became very ill and his ship was driven to an uninhabited follow-up <a href="/wiki/Bering_Island" title="Bering Island">Bering Island</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Commander_Islands" title="Commander Islands">Commander</a> group. Bering died there, along with part of his crew. The rest built a vessel out of the wreckage of <i>Sv. Piotr</i> and escaped to Petropavlovsk.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-britannica11_32-0"><a href="#cite_note-britannica11-32">[32]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Bering_Strait" title="Bering Strait">Bering Strait</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bering_Sea" title="Bering Sea">Bering Sea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bering_Island" title="Bering Island">Bering Island</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bering_Glacier" title="Bering Glacier">Bering Glacier</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bering_Land_Bridge" title="Bering Land Bridge">Bering Land Bridge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Beringia" title="Beringia">Beringia</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Vitus-bering-parken-2005.jpg"><img alt="A plaque in Danish Vitus Bering Park" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="576" data-file-width="720" decoding="async" height="96" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Vitus-bering-parken-2005.jpg/120px-Vitus-bering-parken-2005.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Vitus-bering-parken-2005.jpg/180px-Vitus-bering-parken-2005.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Vitus-bering-parken-2005.jpg/240px-Vitus-bering-parken-2005.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Vitus-bering-parken-2005.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A plaque in <a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Danish</a> Vitus Bering Park with Bering\'s voyages etched</div></div></div></div><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:1966_CPA_3446.jpg"><img alt="Commander Islands and Alaska" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="771" data-file-width="1549" decoding="async" height="60" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/1966_CPA_3446.jpg/120px-1966_CPA_3446.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/1966_CPA_3446.jpg/180px-1966_CPA_3446.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/1966_CPA_3446.jpg/240px-1966_CPA_3446.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:1966_CPA_3446.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A postage stamp depicting the discovery of the <a href="/wiki/Commander_Islands" title="Commander Islands">Commander Islands</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a>.</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#dfdfff;">\n<th scope="row">\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Joseph_Billings" title="Joseph Billings">Joseph Billings</a></b>^<br/>(c. 1758&#8211;1806)<br/><a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a> and Russian Navy officer\n</td>\n<td>In 1785&#8211;95 Billings, previously an English officer who had sailed with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Captain_Cook" title="Captain Cook">Captain Cook</a>, led a Russian expedition in search of the <a href="/wiki/Northeast_Passage" title="Northeast Passage">Northeast Passage</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Gavril_Sarychev" title="Gavril Sarychev">Gavril Sarychev</a> as his deputy. They made accurate maps of the <a href="/wiki/Chukchi_Peninsula" title="Chukchi Peninsula">Chukchi Peninsula</a>, the west coast of <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Aleutian_Islands" title="Aleutian Islands">Aleutian Islands</a>. They landed on <a href="/wiki/Kodiak_Island" title="Kodiak Island">Kodiak Island</a>, examined the area of <a href="/wiki/Prince_William_Sound" title="Prince William Sound">Prince William Sound</a> and compiled a census of the native population of the Aleutians. Billings crossed Chukotka on <a href="/wiki/Reindeer" title="Reindeer">reindeer</a> and made the first elaborate description of the <a href="/wiki/Chukchi_people" title="Chukchi people">Chukchi people</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Cape_Billings" title="Cape Billings">Cape Billings</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Billings_(Chukotka)" title="Billings (Chukotka)">Billings (Chukotka)</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Siberia_CBL.png"><img alt="Cape Billings" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="409" data-file-width="710" decoding="async" height="69" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Siberia_CBL.png/120px-Siberia_CBL.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Siberia_CBL.png/180px-Siberia_CBL.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Siberia_CBL.png/240px-Siberia_CBL.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Siberia_CBL.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Location of <a href="/wiki/Cape_Billings" title="Cape Billings">Cape Billings</a> in Chukotka</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#f0f8ff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Brusilov_Georgy.jpg"><img alt="Brusilov" data-file-height="428" data-file-width="282" decoding="async" height="137" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Brusilov_Georgy.jpg/90px-Brusilov_Georgy.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Brusilov_Georgy.jpg/135px-Brusilov_Georgy.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Brusilov_Georgy.jpg/180px-Brusilov_Georgy.jpg 2x" width="90"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Georgy_Brusilov" title="Georgy Brusilov">Georgy Brusilov</a></b>^<br/>(1884&#8211;1914?)<br/>Russian Navy captain\n</td>\n<td>In 1910&#8211;11, Brusilov took part in a hydrographic expedition on the icebreakers <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Icebreaker_Taymyr" title="Icebreaker Taymyr">Taymyr</a></i> and <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Icebreaker_Vaygach" title="Icebreaker Vaygach">Vaygach</a></i> to the <a href="/wiki/Chukchi_Sea" title="Chukchi Sea">Chukchi</a> and <a href="/wiki/East_Siberian_Sea" title="East Siberian Sea">East Siberian Seas</a>. In 1912&#8211;14 he led an expedition on the brig<i> <a href="/wiki/Svyataya_Anna" title="Svyataya Anna">St.Anna</a></i>, which aimed to travel by the <a href="/wiki/Northern_Sea_Route" title="Northern Sea Route">Northern Sea Route</a> from the Atlantic to the Pacific. <i>St.Anna</i> became icebound west of <a href="/wiki/Yamal_Peninsula" title="Yamal Peninsula">Yamal Peninsula</a> and drifted to the <a href="/wiki/North_Pole" title="North Pole">North Pole</a> in 1913. Brusilov became ill and many of the crew succumbed to scurvy. In 1914 a group led by lieutenant <a href="/wiki/Valerian_Albanov" title="Valerian Albanov">Valerian Albanov</a> abandoned the ship and walked south over the drifting ice. Only Albanov and <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Konrad" title="Alexander Konrad">Alexander Konrad</a> managed to reach <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Franz_Joseph_Land" title="Franz Joseph Land">Franz Joseph Land</a>, where they were rescued by <a href="/wiki/Georgy_Sedov" title="Georgy Sedov">Georgy Sedov</a>\'s <i>St. Foka</i>. The efforts to find the <i>St. Anna</i> were unsuccessful.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-alb_18-1"><a href="#cite_note-alb-18">[18]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Brusilov and his ship are among the prototypes for the novel <i><a href="/wiki/The_Two_Captains" title="The Two Captains">The Two Captains</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Veniamin_Kaverin" title="Veniamin Kaverin">Veniamin Kaverin</a>, where the fictional <i>St. Maria</i> repeats the drift of <i>St. Anna</i>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Kara_Sea_map.png"><img alt="Kara Sea" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="858" data-file-width="942" decoding="async" height="109" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Kara_Sea_map.png/120px-Kara_Sea_map.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Kara_Sea_map.png/180px-Kara_Sea_map.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Kara_Sea_map.png/240px-Kara_Sea_map.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Kara_Sea_map.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Kara_Sea" title="Kara Sea">Kara Sea</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#ffe8d5;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bulatovich.jpg"><img alt="Bulatovich" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Bulatovich.jpg/135px-Bulatovich.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Bulatovich.jpg/180px-Bulatovich.jpg 2x" width="90"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Alexander_Bulatovich" title="Alexander Bulatovich">Alexander Bulatovich</a></b><img alt="dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/37/Dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/>(1870&#8211;1919)<br/>Russian Army officer, writer, hieromonk (tonsured Father Antony), <a href="/wiki/Imiaslavie" title="Imiaslavie">imiaslavie</a> leader, hero of <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a>\n</td>\n<td>In 1897 Bulatovich was a member of the Russian mission of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Red_Cross" title="Red Cross">Red Cross</a> in Africa, where he became a confidant of Negus <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Menelek_II_of_Ethiopia" title="Menelek II of Ethiopia">Menelek II of Ethiopia</a> and his military aide in the war with Italy and the southern tribes. He became the first European to provide a description of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kaffa_Province,_Ethiopia" title="Kaffa Province, Ethiopia">Kaffa province</a> (conquered by Menelek II with Bulatovich\'s help) and among the first to reach the mouth of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Omo_River_(Ethiopia)" title="Omo River (Ethiopia)">Omo River</a>. Among the places named by Bulatovich was the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nicholas_II" title="Nicholas II">Nicholas II</a> Mountain range.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">The prototype for  grotesque Schema-Hussar Alexei Bulanovich in <a href="/wiki/Ilf_and_Petrov" title="Ilf and Petrov">Ilf and Petrov</a>\'s <i><a href="/wiki/The_Twelve_Chairs" title="The Twelve Chairs">The Twelve Chairs</a></i>; the hero of <a href="/wiki/Valentin_Pikul" title="Valentin Pikul">Valentin Pikul</a>\'s <i>The Hussar on a Camel</i> and Richard Seltzer\'s <i>The Name of Hero</i>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ethiopia_shaded_relief_map_1999,_CIA.jpg"><img alt="Ethiopia" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1215" data-file-width="1010" decoding="async" height="144" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Ethiopia_shaded_relief_map_1999%2C_CIA.jpg/120px-Ethiopia_shaded_relief_map_1999%2C_CIA.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Ethiopia_shaded_relief_map_1999%2C_CIA.jpg/180px-Ethiopia_shaded_relief_map_1999%2C_CIA.jpg 1.5x, title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#ffe8d5;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Admiral_Faddey_Faddeyevich_Bellingshausen.jpg/135px-Admiral_Faddey_Faddeyevich_Bellingshausen.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Admiral_Faddey_Faddeyevich_Bellingshausen.jpg/180px-Admiral_Faddey_Faddeyevich_Bellingshausen.jpg 2x" width="90"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Fabian_Gottlieb_von_Bellingshausen" title="Fabian Gottlieb von Bellingshausen">Fabian Bellingshausen</a></b><img alt="dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/37/Dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/>(1878&#8211;1852)<br/> Russian officer of Baltic German descent in the Imperial Russian Navy, cartographer and explorer\n</td>\n<td>The discoverer of the <a href="/wiki/Antarctica" title="Antarctica">Antarctica</a>.\n<p>In 1819 the authorities selected Bellingshausen to lead the First Russian Antarctic Expedition which was intended to explore the Southern Ocean and to find land in the proximity of the South Pole. With two ships, sloop-of-war Vostok ("East") and support vessel Mirny ("Peaceful") were led by <a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Lazarev" title="Mikhail Lazarev">Mikhail Lazarev</a>, the journey started from Kronstadt on 4 June 1819.\nBellingshausen and Lazarev managed to twice circumnavigate the continent. Thus they disproved Captain Cook\'s assertion that it was impossible to find land in the southern ice fields. The expedition also made discoveries and observations in the tropical waters of the Pacific Ocean.\n</p>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bellingshausen-fr.svg"><img alt="First Russian Antarctic Expedition 1819-1821" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="621" data-file-width="503" decoding="async" height="148" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Bellingshausen-fr.svg/120px-Bellingshausen-fr.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Bellingshausen-fr.svg/180px-Bellingshausen-fr.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Bellingshausen-fr.svg/240px-Bellingshausen-fr.svg.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Bellingshausen-fr.svg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>First Russian Antarctic Expedition 1819-1821</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" C">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div aria-labelledby="tocheading" class="toc plainlinks hlist" id="toc" role="navigation" style="text-align:left;">\n<div width="22%">Person\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="60%">Achievements\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Image\n</th></tr>\n<tr style="background:#f0f8ff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:RR5111-0030R.gif"><img alt="Chelyuskin" data-file-height="271" data-file-width="271" decoding="async" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/RR5111-0030R.gif/120px-RR5111-0030R.gif" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/RR5111-0030R.gif/180px-RR5111-0030R.gif 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/RR5111-0030R.gif/240px-RR5111-0030R.gif 2x" width="120"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Semion_Chelyuskin" title="Semion Chelyuskin">Semion Chelyuskin</a></b><img alt="double-dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/>(c. 1700&#8211;1764)<br/>Russian Navy officer<br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">(<a href="/wiki/Stepan_Malygin" title="Stepan Malygin">Malygin</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/D._Ovtsyn" title="D. Ovtsyn">D. Ovtsyn</a>, <b>Chelyuskin</b>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kh._Laptev" title="Kh. Laptev">Kh. Laptev</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/D._Laptev" title="D. Laptev">D. Laptev</a> on a commemorative coin)</span>\n</td>\n<td>Chelyuskin participated in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Northern_Expedition" title="Great Northern Expedition">Great Northern Expedition</a> in 1733&#8211;43. He traveled in the groups led by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vasily_Pronchischev" title="Vasily Pronchischev">Vasily Pronchischev</a> and <a href="/wiki/Khariton_Laptev" title="Khariton Laptev">Khariton Laptev</a>. In 1741 he led his own voyage from the <a href="/wiki/Khatanga_River" title="Khatanga River">Khatanga River</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Pyasina_River" title="Pyasina River">Pyasina River</a> by land. He explored and described the western coastline of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Taimyr_Peninsula" title="Taimyr Peninsula">Taimyr Peninsula</a> and the mouths of Pyasina and <a href="/wiki/Yenisei_River" title="Yenisei River">Yenisei Rivers</a>. In 1741&#8211;42, he traveled from <a href="/wiki/Turukhansk" title="Turukhansk">Turukhansk</a> to the mouth of the Khatanga and described the northern coastline of Taimyr from Cape Faddey in the east to the mouth of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Taimyra_River" title="Taimyra River">Taimyra River</a> in the west. Chelyuskin discovered the northern extremity of <a href="/wiki/Asia" title="Asia">Asia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cape_Chelyuskin" title="Cape Chelyuskin">Cape Chelyuskin</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pronchiscev-chelyuskin_38-0"><a href="#cite_note-pronchiscev-chelyuskin-38">[38]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Cape_Chelyuskin" title="Cape Chelyuskin">Cape Chelyuskin</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chelyuskin_Peninsula" title="Chelyuskin Peninsula">Chelyuskin Peninsula</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chelyuskin_Island" title="Chelyuskin Island">Chelyuskin Island</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chelyuskin_steamship" title="Chelyuskin steamship">Chelyuskin steamship</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Kara_sea2CC.PNG"><img alt="Cape Chelyuskin" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="534" data-file-width="701" decoding="async" height="91" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Kara_sea2CC.PNG/120px-Kara_sea2CC.PNG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Kara_sea2CC.PNG/180px-Kara_sea2CC.PNG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Kara_sea2CC.PNG/240px-Kara_sea2CC.PNG 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Kara_sea2CC.PNG" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Cape_Chelyuskin" title="Cape Chelyuskin">Cape Chelyuskin</a>, the northernmost point of <a href="/wiki/Eurasia" title="Eurasia">Eurasia</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#dfffdf;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Jan_Czerski.jpg"><img alt="Chersky" data-file-height="400" data-file-width="322" decoding="async" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Jan_Czerski.jpg/100px-Jan_Czerski.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Jan_Czerski.jpg/150px-Jan_Czerski.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Jan_Czerski.jpg/200px-Jan_Czerski.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ivan_Chersky" title="Ivan Chersky">Ivan Chersky</a></b>*<br/>(1845&#8211;1892)<br/>paleontologist, geologist, geographer\n</td>\n<td>Exiled to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Transbaikalia" title="Transbaikalia">Transbaikalia</a> for participation in the <a href="/wiki/January_Uprising" title="January Uprising">January Uprising</a> and pardoned only in 1883, Chersky became a self-taught scientist in <a href="/wiki/Siberia" title="Siberia">Siberia</a>. He traveled to the <a href="/wiki/Sayan_Mountains" title="Sayan Mountains">Sayan Mountains</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Irkut_River" title="Irkut River">Irkut River</a> Valley and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lower_Tunguska" title="Lower Tunguska">Lower Tunguska</a>. During four expeditions in 1877&#8211;81 Chersky explored <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Selenga" title="Selenga">Selenga</a> river. He explained the origin of <a href="/wiki/Lake_Baikal" title="Lake Baikal">Lake Baikal</a>, made the first geological map of its coast and described the geological structure of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/East_Siberia" title="East Siberia">East Siberia</a>. He analysed the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tectonic" title="Tectonic">tectonics</a> of Inner Asia and pioneered the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Geomorphological" title="Geomorphological">geomorphological</a> evolution theory. He collected over 2,500 ancient bones. In 1892 he explored the <a href="/wiki/Kolyma" title="Kolyma">Kolyma</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yana_River" title="Yana River">Yana</a> and <a href="/wiki/Indigirka_River" title="Indigirka River">Indigirka Rivers</a> and died from illness there.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rfe_39-0"><a href="#cite_note-Rfe-39">[39]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Chersky_Range" title="Chersky Range">Chersky Range</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chersky_(settlement)" title="Chersky (settlement)">Chersky (settlement)</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Selengerivermap.png"><img alt="Selenga watershed" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="500" decoding="async" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Selengerivermap.png/120px-Selengerivermap.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Selengerivermap.png/180px-Selengerivermap.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Selengerivermap.png/240px-Selengerivermap.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Selengerivermap.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Selenga" title="Selenga">Selenga</a> watershed</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#f0f8ff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Chichagov.jpg"><img alt="Chichagov" data-file-height="423" data-file-width="360" decoding="async" height="118" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c2/Chichagov.jpg/100px-Chichagov.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c2/Chichagov.jpg/150px-Chichagov.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c2/Chichagov.jpg/200px-Chichagov.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vasili_Chichagov" title="Vasili Chichagov">Vasili Chichagov</a></b><img alt="double-dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/>(1726&#8211;1809)<br/>Russian admiral, victorious commander-in-chief of the <a href="/wiki/Baltic_Fleet" title="Baltic Fleet">Baltic Fleet</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Russo-Swedish_War_(1788%E2%80%931790)" title="Russo-Swedish War (1788&#8211;1790)">Russo-Swedish War (1788&#8211;1790)</a>\n</td>\n<td>In 1764&#8211;66 Chichagov led two expeditions to find the <a href="/wiki/Northeast_Passage" title="Northeast Passage">Northeast Passage</a> between the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Atlantic" title="Atlantic">Atlantic</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pacific" title="Pacific">Pacific</a> along the northern coast of <a href="/wiki/Siberia" title="Siberia">Siberia</a>, a project of <a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Lomonosov" title="Mikhail Lomonosov">Mikhail Lomonosov</a>. Although he sailed past <a href="/wiki/Svalbard" title="Svalbard">Svalbard</a>, reached 80&#176;26\'N in 1765 and 80&#176;30\'N in 1766, and conducted valuable research, both expeditions failed to find the route.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Chichagof_Island" title="Chichagof Island">Chichagof Island</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Barents_Sea_map.png"><img alt="Barents and Baltic Seas" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1084" data-file-width="1187" decoding="async" height="110" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Barents_Sea_map.png/120px-Barents_Sea_map.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Barents_Sea_map.png/180px-Barents_Sea_map.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Barents_Sea_map.png/240px-Barents_Sea_map.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Barents_Sea_map.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Barents_Sea" title="Barents Sea">Barents</a> and <a href="/wiki/Baltic_Sea" title="Baltic Sea">Baltic Seas</a>, where Chichagov explored and fought</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#ffffd0;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pjotr_Alexandrowitsch_Tschichatschow.jpeg"><img alt="Chikhachyov" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="350" decoding="async" height="129" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/Pjotr_Alexandrowitsch_Tschichatschow.jpeg/90px-Pjotr_Alexandrowitsch_Tschichatschow.jpeg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/Pjotr_Alexandrowitsch_Tschichatschow.jpeg/135px-Pjotr_Alexandrowitsch_Tschichatschow.jpeg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/Pjotr_Alexandrowitsch_Tschichatschow.jpeg/180px-Pjotr_Alexandrowitsch_Tschichatschow.jpeg 2x" width="90"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Pyotr_Chikhachyov" title="Pyotr Chikhachyov">Pyotr Chikhachyov</a></b>!<br/>(1808&#8211;1890)<br/>naturalist, geologist\n</td>\n<td>In 1842 Chikhachyov led an expedition to the unknown territories of the Altai and <a href="/wiki/Sayan_Mountains" title="Sayan Mountains">Sayan Mountains</a>. He discovered <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kuznetsk_Coal_Basin" title="Kuznetsk Coal Basin">Kuznetsk Coal Basin</a>, reached the sources of the rivers <a href="/wiki/Abakan" title="Abakan">Abakan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chu_River" title="Chu River">Chu</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chulyshman" title="Chulyshman">Chulyshman</a>, and entered <a href="/wiki/Tuva" title="Tuva">Tuva</a>. In 1845 he published works on the geology of <a href="/wiki/Altai_Mountains" title="Altai Mountains">Altai Mountains</a> and <a href="/wiki/Xinjiang" title="Xinjiang">Xinjiang</a>. In 1848&#8211;63 he led eight expeditions in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Asia_Minor" title="Asia Minor">Asia Minor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Armenia" title="Armenia">Armenia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kurdistan" title="Kurdistan">Kurdistan</a> and <a href="/wiki/East_Thrace" title="East Thrace">East Thrace</a>. In 1853&#8211;69 he conducted a major study of Asia Minor, while being the attach&#233; of the Russian embassy in <a href="/wiki/Constantinople" title="Constantinople">Constantinople</a>. In 1878, at the age of 71, he visited Algeria and Tunis. He published many works in geography, natural history and the politics of the <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Question" title="Eastern Question">Eastern Question</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Altay-Sayan_map_en.png"><img alt="Mountains of Central Asia" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="330" data-file-width="750" decoding="async" height="53" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Altay-Sayan_map_en.png/120px-Altay-Sayan_map_en.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Altay-Sayan_map_en.png/180px-Altay-Sayan_map_en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Altay-Sayan_map_en.png/240px-Altay-Sayan_map_en.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Altay-Sayan_map_en.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mountains of <a href="/wiki/Central_Asia" title="Central Asia">Central Asia</a></div></div></div></div><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Turkey_topo.jpg"><img alt="Asia Minor" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="752" title="Asia Minor">Asia Minor</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#f0f8ff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Chilingarov_Arh.jpg"><img alt="Chilingarov" data-file-height="3264" data-file-width="2312" decoding="async" height="127" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Chilingarov_Arh.jpg/90px-Chilingarov_Arh.jpg" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Chilingarov_Arh.jpg/180px-Chilingarov_Arh.jpg 2x" width="90"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Artur_Chilingarov" title="Artur Chilingarov">Artur Chilingarov</a></b><img alt="double-dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/>(born 1939)<br/>polar scientist, <a href="/wiki/Hero_of_the_Soviet_Union" title="Hero of the Soviet Union">Hero of the Soviet Union</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hero_of_Russia" title="Hero of Russia">Hero of Russia</a>, politician\n</td>\n<td>In 1969 Chilingarov became the head of the research station "<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/North_Pole-19" title="North Pole-19">North Pole-19</a>" and in 1971 the head of <a href="/wiki/Bellingshausen_Station" title="Bellingshausen Station">Bellingshausen Station</a> during the 17-th <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Antarctic_Expedition" title="Soviet Antarctic Expedition">Soviet Antarctic Expedition</a>. In 1985 he successfully led the mission to rescue the research vessel <i><a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Somov" title="Mikhail Somov">Mikhail Somov</a></i>, which had been ice-blocked in the <a href="/wiki/Southern_Ocean" title="Southern Ocean">Southern Ocean</a>. During the Russian <a href="/wiki/Arktika_2007" title="Arktika 2007">Arktika 2007</a> expedition, Chilingarov, accompanied by other explorers from different countries, descended to the seabed 13,980&#160;feet below the <a href="/wiki/North_Pole" title="North Pole">North Pole</a> in order to plant  the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russian_flag" title="Russian flag">Russian flag</a> there and gather specimens of the bottom ground, using <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MIR_submersible" title="MIR submersible">MIR submersibles</a>. In 2008 he took part in the expedition which descended one mile to the bottom of <a href="/wiki/Lake_Baikal" title="Lake Baikal">Lake Baikal</a> on MIRs.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-chilingarov_17-1"><a href="#cite_note-chilingarov-17">[17]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mir_front.jpg"><img alt="MIR submersible" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2272" data-file-width="1704" decoding="async" height="160" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Mir_front.jpg/120px-Mir_front.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Mir_front.jpg/180px-Mir_front.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Mir_front.jpg/240px-Mir_front.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" style="background:#dfdfff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tschirikow.jpg"><img alt="Chirikov" data-file-height="351" data-file-width="296" decoding="async" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Tschirikow.jpg/180px-Tschirikow.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Tschirikow.jpg/240px-Tschirikow.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Aleksei_Chirikov" title="Aleksei Chirikov">Aleksei Chirikov</a></b>^<br/>(1703&#8211;1748) <br/>Russian Navy captain\n</td>\n<td>In 1725&#8211;30 and in 1733&#8211;43, Chirikov was <a href="/wiki/Vitus_Bering" title="Vitus Bering">Vitus Bering</a>\'s deputy during the 1st and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2nd_Kamchatka_expedition" title="2nd Kamchatka expedition">2nd Kamchatka expeditions</a>. On July 15, 1741 Chirikov, the captain of <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Paul_of_Tarsus" title="Paul of Tarsus">Sv. Pavel</a></i>, became the first European to land on the northwestern coast of <a href="/wiki/North_America" title="North America">North America</a> near <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Archipelago" title="Alexander Archipelago">Alexander Archipelago</a>. Thereafter he discovered some of the <a href="/wiki/Aleutian_Islands" title="Aleutian Islands">Aleutian Islands</a>. In 1742 Chirikov specified the location of the <a href="/wiki/Attu_Island" title="Attu Island">Attu Island</a> during the search for Bering\'s lost ship. In 1746 Chirikov took part in creating the final map of the Russian discoveries in the northern <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific Ocean</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Chirikof_Island" title="Chirikof Island">Chirikof Island</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Alexander_archipelago.jpg"><img alt="Alexander Archipelago" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1400" data-file-width="1050" decoding="async" height="160" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Alexander_archipelago.jpg/120px-Alexander_archipelago.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Alexander_archipelago.jpg/180px-Alexander_archipelago.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Alexander_archipelago.jpg/240px-Alexander_archipelago.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Alexander_archipelago.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Alexander_Archipelago" title="Alexander Archipelago">Alexander Archipelago</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#f0f8ff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Chkalov_1937.jpg"><img alt="Chkalov" data-file-height="755" data-file-width="500" decoding="async" height="151" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Chkalov_1937.jpg/100px-Chkalov_1937.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Chkalov_1937.jpg/150px-Chkalov_1937.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Chkalov_1937.jpg/200px-Chkalov_1937.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Valery_Chkalov" title="Valery Chkalov">Valery Chkalov</a></b><img alt="double-dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/>(1904&#8211;1938)<br/>military and test pilot, Hero of the Soviet Union\n</td>\n<td>Chkalov developed several new figures of <a href="/wiki/Aerobatics" title="Aerobatics">aerobatics</a>. He was involved in a number of <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet</a> ultralong flights. In 1936 Chkalov, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Georgiy_Baidukov" title="Georgiy Baidukov">Georgiy Baidukov</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Vasilyevich_Belyakov" title="Alexander Vasilyevich Belyakov">A.V.Belyakov</a> on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ANT-25" title="ANT-25">ANT-25</a> flew 9,374&#160;km from <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> through the <a href="/wiki/North_Pole" title="North Pole">North Pole</a> to follow-up <a href="/wiki/Chkalov_Island" title="Chkalov Island">Chkalov Island</a> in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Okhotsk_Sea" title="Okhotsk Sea">Okhotsk Sea</a>, which took 56 h 20&#160;min. In 1937, also on ANT-25, the same crew flew 8,504&#160;km from Moscow through the North Pole to <a href="/wiki/Vancouver,_Washington" title="Vancouver, Washington">Vancouver, Washington</a>, which was the first transpolar flight between <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a> and <a href="/wiki/North_America" title="North America">North America</a> on airplane, rather than on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dirigible" title="Dirigible">dirigible</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Chkalovsk,_Russia" title="Chkalovsk, Russia">Chkalovsk</a>; <a href="/wiki/Chkalov_Island" title="Chkalov Island">Chkalov Island</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chkalovskaya_(Moscow_Metro)" title="Chkalovskaya (Moscow Metro)">Chkalovskaya (Moscow Metro)</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chkalovskaya_(Saint_Petersburg_Metro)" title="Chkalovskaya (Saint Petersburg Metro)">Chkalovskaya (Saint Petersburg Metro)</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:URSS_ANT-25_N025_in_flight.jpg"><img alt="ANT-25" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="215" data-file-width="400" decoding="async" height="65" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/URSS_ANT-25_N025_in_flight.jpg/240px-URSS_ANT-25_N025_in_flight.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:URSS_ANT-25_N025_in_flight.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ANT-25" title="ANT-25">ANT-25</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="D">D</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Russian_explorers&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: D">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div width="22%">Person\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="60%">Achievements\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Image\n</th></tr>\n<tr style="background:#dfdfff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Semyon_Dezhnyov_by_Brodsky.jpg"><img alt="Dezhnyov" data-file-height="334" data-file-width="300" decoding="async" height="122" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Semyon_Dezhnyov_by_Brodsky.jpg/110px-Semyon_Dezhnyov_by_Brodsky.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Semyon_Dezhnyov_by_Brodsky.jpg/165px-Semyon_Dezhnyov_by_Brodsky.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Semyon_Dezhnyov_by_Brodsky.jpg/220px-Semyon_Dezhnyov_by_Brodsky.jpg 2x" width="110"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Semyon_Dezhnyov" title="Semyon Dezhnyov">Semyon Dezhnyov</a></b>^<br/>(c. 1605&#8211;1672)<br/><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Siberian_Cossack" title="Siberian Cossack">Siberian Cossack</a> leader\n</td>\n<td>In 1643 Dezhnyov and <a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Stadukhin" title="Mikhail Stadukhin">Mikhail Stadukhin</a> discovered the <a href="/wiki/Kolyma_River" title="Kolyma River">Kolyma River</a> and founded <a href="/wiki/Srednekolymsk" title="Srednekolymsk">Srednekolymsk</a>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fedot_Alekseyev_Popov" title="Fedot Alekseyev Popov">Fedot Alekseyev Popov</a> organized a further expedition eastward, and Dezhnyov became a captain of one <a href="/wiki/Koch_(boat)" title="Koch (boat)">koch</a>. In 1648 they sailed from Srednekolymsk down to the <a href="/wiki/Arctic" title="Arctic">Arctic</a> and after some time they rounded a<i> \'<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cape_Dezhnyov" title="Cape Dezhnyov">great rocky projection</a>\', </i>thus becoming the first to pass through the <a href="/wiki/Bering_Strait" title="Bering Strait">Bering Strait</a> and to discover <a href="/wiki/Chukchi_Peninsula" title="Chukchi Peninsula">Chukchi Peninsula</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Bering_Sea" title="Bering Sea">Bering Sea</a>. All their kochi and most of their men (including Popov himself) were lost in storms and clashes with the natives. A small group led by Dezhnyov reached the mouth of the <a href="/wiki/Anadyr_River" title="Anadyr River">Anadyr River</a> and sailed up it in 1649, having built new boats out of the wreckage. They founded <a href="/wiki/Anadyrsk" title="Anadyrsk">Anadyrsk</a> and were stranded there, until Stadukhin found them, coming from Kolyma by land.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rfisher_44-0"><a href="#cite_note-rfisher-44">[44]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cape_Dezhnyov" title="Cape Dezhnyov">Cape Dezhnyov</a> (the easternmost cape of <a href="/wiki/Eurasia" title="Eurasia">Eurasia</a>).</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Anadyrrivermap.png"><img alt="Bering Strait" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="500" decoding="async" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/Anadyrrivermap.png/120px-Anadyrrivermap.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/Anadyrrivermap.png/180px-Anadyrrivermap.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/Anadyrrivermap.png/240px-Anadyrrivermap.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Anadyrrivermap.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Bering_Strait" title="Bering Strait">Bering Strait</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Anadyr_River" title="Anadyr River">Anadyr River</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#fff8e7;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%D0%94%D0%BE%D0%BA%D1%83%D1%87%D0%B0%D0%B5%D0%B2,_%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D1%8C%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87.jpg"><img alt="Dokuchaev" 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/%D0%94%D0%BE%D0%BA%D1%83%D1%87%D0%B0%D0%B5%D0%B2%2C_%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D1%8C%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87.jpg/200px-%D0%94%D0%BE%D0%BA%D1%83%D1%87%D0%B0%D0%B5%D0%B2%2C_%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D1%8C%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Vasily_Dokuchaev" title="Vasily Dokuchaev">Vasily Dokuchaev</a></b>~<br/>(1846&#8211;1903)<br/>geographer, geologist, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pedology_(soil_study)" title="Pedology (soil study)">pedologist</a>\n</td>\n<td>Dokuchaev led numerous expeditions to study the <a href="/wiki/Soil" title="Soil">soils</a> and geology of <a href="/wiki/European_Russia" title="European Russia">European Russia</a>. As a result of his long research of Russian soils, he founded modern <a href="/wiki/Soil_science" title="Soil science">soil science</a>, developed the conception of <a href="/wiki/Biome" title="Biome">biomes</a> and proposed ways to improve soil productivity.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rbd_19-1"><a href="#cite_note-rbd-19">[19]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dokuchaevsk" title="Dokuchaevsk">Dokuchaevsk</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Global_soil_regions.jpg"><img alt="Global soil regions" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="574" data-file-width="740" decoding="async" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Global_soil_regions.jpg/120px-Global_soil_regions.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Global_soil_regions.jpg/180px-Global_soil_regions.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Global_soil_regions.jpg/240px-Global_soil_regions.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Global_soil_regions.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Global <a href="/wiki/Soil_classification" title="Soil classification">soil regions</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="E">E</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Russian_explorers&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: E">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div aria-labelledby="tocheading" class="toc plainlinks hlist" id="toc" role="navigation" style="text-align:left;">\n<div class="toctitle" id="toctitle" style="text-align:center;display:inline-block;"><span id="tocheading" style="font-weight:bold;">Contents:&#160;</span></div>\n<div style="margin:auto;white-space:nowrap;display:inline-block;">\n<ul><li><a href="#top">Top</a></li>\n<li><a href="#0&#8211;9">0&#8211;9</a></li>\n<li><a href="#A">A</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/File:Arvid_Adolf_Ethol%C3%A9n.jpg"><img alt="Ethol&#233;n" data-file-height="227" data-file-width="181" decoding="async" height="125" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Arvid_Adolf_Ethol%C3%A9n.jpg/150px-Arvid_Adolf_Ethol%C3%A9n.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/2/29/Arvid_Adolf_Ethol%C3%A9n.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Arvid_Adolf_Ethol%C3%A9n" title="Arvid Adolf Ethol&#233;n">Arvid Adolf Ethol&#233;n</a></b>^<br/>(1799&#8211;1876)<br/>Russian Navy officer, colonial administrator\n</td>\n<td>Etolin sailed to <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a> with <a href="/wiki/Vasily_Golovnin" title="Vasily Golovnin">Vasily Golovnin</a> on <i><a href="/wiki/Russian_frigate_Kamchatka" title="Russian frigate Kamchatka">Kamchatka</a></i> and entered the service of the <a href="/wiki/Russian-American_Company" title="Russian-American Company">Russian-American Company</a>. He was part of a group that surveyed the <a href="/wiki/Aleutian_Islands" title="Aleutian Islands">Aleutian Islands</a> in 1822&#8211;24. In 1833 he explored the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Alaska" title="Gulf of Alaska">Gulf of Alaska</a>. Etolin was the governor of <a href="/wiki/Russian_America" title="Russian America">Russian America</a> in 1840&#8211;45, and continued to explore Alaska and the <a href="/wiki/Bering_Sea" title="Bering Sea">Bering Sea</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Etolin_Island" title="Etolin Island">Etolin Island</a>, <a href="/wiki/Etolin_Strait" title="Etolin Strait">Etolin Strait</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Aleuten_Lage.png"><img alt="Aleutian Islands" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="545" data-file-width="707" decoding="async" 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Aleuten_Lage.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Aleutian_Islands" title="Aleutian Islands">Aleutian Islands</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#ffffd0;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Eduard_Eversmann.jpg"><img alt="Eversmann" data-file-height="200" data-file-width="150" decoding="async" height="133" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/d/df/Eduard_Eversmann.jpg/100px-Eduard_Eversmann.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/d/df/Eduard_Eversmann.jpg 1.5x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Eduard_Friedrich_Eversmann" title="Eduard Friedrich Eversmann">Eduard Eversmann</a></b>!<br/>(1794&#8211;1860)<br/>naturalist\n</td>\n<td>In 1820 Eversmann traveled to <a href="/wiki/Bukhara" title="Bukhara">Bukhara</a> disguised as a merchant and in 1825 traveled with a military expedition to <a href="/wiki/Khiva" title="Khiva">Khiva</a>. In 1828 he became a professor of <a href="/wiki/Zoology" title="Zoology">zoology</a> and <a href="/wiki/Botany" title="Botany">botany</a> at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/University_of_Kazan" title="University of Kazan">University of Kazan</a>. He wrote numerous publications and pioneered the research of the flora and fauna of the southeast steppes of Russia between the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Volga" title="Volga">Volga</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Urals" title="Urals">Urals</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46"><a href="#cite_note-46">[46]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Eversmann%27s_redstart" title="Eversmann\'s redstart">Eversmann\'s redstart</a>,  <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eversmann%27s_parnassian" title="Eversmann\'s parnassian">Eversmann\'s parnassian</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eversmann%27s_rustic" title="Eversmann\'s rustic">Eversmann\'s rustic</a> and other species.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:KhivaWalls.jpg"><img alt="Walls of Itchan Kala in Khiva" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1179" data-file-width="1772" decoding="async" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/KhivaWalls.jpg/120px-KhivaWalls.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/KhivaWalls.jpg/180px-KhivaWalls.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/KhivaWalls.jpg/240px-KhivaWalls.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:KhivaWalls.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Walls of <a href="/wiki/Itchan_Kala" title="Itchan Kala">Itchan Kala</a> in <a href="/wiki/Khiva" title="Khiva">Khiva</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="F">F</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Russian_explorers&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: F">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div aria-labelledby="tocheading" class="toc plainlinks hlist" id="toc" role="navigation" style="text-align:left;">\n<div class="toctitle" id="toctitle" style="text-align:center;display:inline-block;"><span id="tocheading" style="font-weight:bold;">Contents:&#160;</span></div>\n<div width="22%">Person\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="60%">Achievements\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Image\n</th></tr>\n<tr style="background:#ffffd0;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Alexei_Fedchenko.jpg/100px-Alexei_Fedchenko.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Alexei_Fedchenko.jpg/150px-Alexei_Fedchenko.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Alexei_Fedchenko.jpg/200px-Alexei_Fedchenko.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Alexei_Pavlovich_Fedchenko" title="Alexei Pavlovich Fedchenko">Alexei Fedchenko</a></b>!<br/>(1844&#8211;1873)<br/>naturalist\n</td>\n<td>In 1868 Fedchenko traveled through <a href="/wiki/Turkestan" title="Turkestan">Turkestan</a>, including <a href="/wiki/Samarkand" title="Samarkand">Samarkand</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Panjkent" title="Panjkent">Panjkent</a> and the upper <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zarafshan_River" title="Zarafshan River">Zarafshan River</a> valley. In 1870 he explored the Fan Mountains south of the Zarafshan. In 1871 he reached the <a href="/wiki/Alay_Valley" title="Alay Valley">Alay Valley</a> at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Daroot-Korgan" title="Daroot-Korgan">Daroot-Korgan</a> and explored the northern <a href="/wiki/Pamir_Mountains" title="Pamir Mountains">Pamir Mountains</a> but was unable to penetrate southward. He perished on <a href="/wiki/Mont_Blanc" title="Mont Blanc">Mont Blanc</a> while engaged in an exploring tour in France.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-britannica11_32-1"><a href="#cite_note-britannica11-32">[32]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47"><a href="#cite_note-47">[47]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Fedchenko_Glacier" title="Fedchenko Glacier">Fedchenko Glacier</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/3195_Fedchenko" title="3195 Fedchenko">3195 Fedchenko</a> (asteroid).</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Location_map_Pamir_mhn.svg"><img alt="Pamir Mountains" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="681" data-file-width="1399" decoding="async" height="58" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Location_map_Pamir_mhn.svg/120px-Location_map_Pamir_mhn.svg.png" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Location_map_Pamir_mhn.svg/240px-Location_map_Pamir_mhn.svg.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Location_map_Pamir_mhn.svg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Pamir_Mountains" title="Pamir Mountains">Pamir Mountains</a> in <a href="/wiki/Central_Asia" title="Central Asia">Central Asia</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#fff8e7;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:1966_CPA_3343.jpg"><img alt="Fersman" data-file-height="889" data-file-width="640" decoding="async" height="139" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/1966_CPA_3343.jpg/100px-1966_CPA_3343.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/1966_CPA_3343.jpg/150px-1966_CPA_3343.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/1966_CPA_3343.jpg/200px-1966_CPA_3343.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Alexander_Fersman" title="Alexander Fersman">Alexander Fersman</a></b>~<br/>(1883&#8211;1945)<br/>geologist, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Geochemist" title="Geochemist">geochemist</a>\n</td>\n<td>Fersman founded <a href="/wiki/Geochemistry" title="Geochemistry">geochemistry</a>, the science of the chemical composition of the <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">Earth</a>. He led numerous expeditions in <a href="/wiki/Crimea" title="Crimea">Crimea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kola_Peninsula" title="Kola Peninsula">Kola Peninsula</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Urals" title="Urals">Urals</a>. He discovered <a href="/wiki/Copper" title="Copper">copper</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nickel" title="Nickel">nickel</a> in <a href="/wiki/Monchegorsk" title="Monchegorsk">Monchegorsk</a>, <a href="/wiki/Apatite" title="Apatite">apatite</a> reserves in <a href="/wiki/Khibiny_Mountains" title="Khibiny Mountains">Khibiny</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sulfur" title="Sulfur">sulfur</a> in <a href="/wiki/Central_Asia" title="Central Asia">Central Asia</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48"><a href="#cite_note-48">[48]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Fersman_Mineralogical_Museum" title="Fersman Mineralogical Museum">Fersman Mineralogical Museum</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fersman_crater" title="Fersman crater">Fersman crater</a> (<a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">Moon</a>).</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Khibiny_North_Rischorr_Pass_1.jpg"><img alt="Khibiny Mountains" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2325" data-file-width="3500" decoding="async" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Khibiny_North_Rischorr_Pass_1.jpg/120px-Khibiny_North_Rischorr_Pass_1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Khibiny_North_Rischorr_Pass_1.jpg/180px-Khibiny_North_Rischorr_Pass_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Khibiny_North_Rischorr_Pass_1.jpg/240px-Khibiny_North_Rischorr_Pass_1.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Khibiny_North_Rischorr_Pass_1.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Khibiny_Mountains" title="Khibiny Mountains">Khibiny Mountains</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#dfdfff;">\n<th scope="row">\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Ivan_Fyodorov_(navigator)" title="Ivan Fyodorov (navigator)">Ivan Fyodorov</a></b>^<br/>(?&#8211;1733)<br/>Russian Navy officer\n</td>\n<td>Fyodorov, took part in the first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kamchatka" title="Kamchatka">Kamchatka</a> expedition of <a href="/wiki/Vitus_Bering" title="Vitus Bering">Vitus Bering</a> in 1725&#8211;30. In 1732 Fyodorov and geodesist <a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Gvozdev" title="Mikhail Gvozdev">Mikhail Gvozdev</a> aboard the <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Gabriel" title="St. Gabriel">Sviatoi Gavriil</a></i> (Bering\'s ship) sailed to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cape_Dezhnyov" title="Cape Dezhnyov">Cape Dezhnyov</a>, the easternmost point of <a href="/wiki/Asia" title="Asia">Asia</a>. From there they sailed east and soon discovered the <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaskan</a> mainland near the <a href="/wiki/Cape_Prince_of_Wales" title="Cape Prince of Wales">Cape Prince of Wales</a>, the westernmost point of <a href="/wiki/North_America" title="North America">North America</a>. They charted the north-western coast of Alaska. By doing this, Fyodorov and Gvozdev completed the discovery of the <a href="/wiki/Bering_Strait" title="Bering Strait">Bering Strait</a>, started by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Semyon_Dezhnyov" title="Semyon Dezhnyov">Semyon Dezhnyov</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fedot_Popov" title="Fedot Popov">Fedot Popov</a> and continued by Bering. Their expedition also discovered three previously unknown islands.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49"><a href="#cite_note-49">[49]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Seward_peninsula.png"><img alt="Cape Prince of Wales area" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="331" data-file-width="583" decoding="async" height="68" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Seward_peninsula.png/120px-Seward_peninsula.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Seward_peninsula.png/180px-Seward_peninsula.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Seward_peninsula.png/240px-Seward_peninsula.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Seward_peninsula.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Seward_Peninsula" title="Seward Peninsula">Seward Peninsula</a> on <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a>, where the <a href="/wiki/Cape_Prince_of_Wales" title="Cape Prince of Wales">Cape Prince of Wales</a> is located</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#dfdfff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hampus-Furuhjelm-1859.jpg"><img alt="Furuhjelm" data-file-height="730" data-file-width="559" decoding="async" height="131" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Hampus-Furuhjelm-1859.jpg/100px-Hampus-Furuhjelm-1859.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Hampus-Furuhjelm-1859.jpg/150px-Hampus-Furuhjelm-1859.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Hampus-Furuhjelm-1859.jpg/200px-Hampus-Furuhjelm-1859.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Johan_Hampus_Furuhjelm" title="Johan Hampus Furuhjelm">Johan Hampus Furuhjelm</a></b>^<br/>(1821&#8211;1909)<br/>Russian admiral, governor of the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Far_East" title="Russian Far East">Russian Far East</a>, <a href="/wiki/Taganrog" title="Taganrog">Taganrog</a> and <a href="/wiki/Russian_America" title="Russian America">Russian America</a><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">(in photo with his wife Anna)</span>\n</td>\n<td>In 1850 Furuhjelm became a commander of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Novoarkhangelsk" title="Novoarkhangelsk">Novoarkhangelsk</a> port (now <a href="/wiki/Sitka,_Alaska" title="Sitka, Alaska">Sitka</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a>) and in 1854 of <a href="/wiki/Ayan,_Russia" title="Ayan, Russia">Ayan</a> port. In 1858&#8211;64 he was the governor of <a href="/wiki/Russian_America" title="Russian America">Russian America</a>. He improved relations with natives, once using the <a href="/wiki/Christopher_Columbus" title="Christopher Columbus">Columbus</a>-like trick of an eclipse of the moon to impress the Indians. In 1865&#8211;72 Furuhjelm served as military governor of <a href="/wiki/Primorsky_Krai" title="Primorsky Krai">Primorsky Krai</a> and chief of Russian seaports on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pacific" title="Pacific">Pacific</a>, where he contributed significantly to the development and exploration of the whole region.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50"><a href="#cite_note-50">[50]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Mount_Furuhelm" title="Mount Furuhelm">Mount Furuhelm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Furugelm_Island" title="Furugelm Island">Furugelm Island</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:1860-russian-america.jpg"><img alt="Russian America" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="831" data-file-width="732" decoding="async" height="136" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/1860-russian-america.jpg/120px-1860-russian-america.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/1860-russian-america.jpg/180px-1860-russian-america.jpg 1.5x, href="/wiki/File:1860-russian-america.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Russian_America" title="Russian America">Russian America</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="G">G</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Russian_explorers&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: G">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div aria-labelledby="tocheading" class="toc plainlinks hlist" id="toc" role="navigation" style="text-align:left;">\n<div class="toctitle" id="toctitle" style="text-align:center;display:inline-block;"><span id="tocheading" style="font-weight:bold;">Contents:&#160;</span></div>\n<div style="margin:auto;white-space:nowrap;display:inline-block;">\n<ul><li><a href="#top">Top</a></li>\n<li><a href="#0&#8211;9">0&#8211;9</a></li>\n<li><a href="#A">A</a></li>\n<li><a
