</li></ul>\n<p class="mw-empty-elt">\n</p>\n</div></div>\n<table class="wikitable">\n<tbody><tr style="background:#ccc;">\n<th scope="col" width="18%">Portrait\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="22%">Person\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="60%">Achievements\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Image\n</th></tr>\n<tr style="background:#FFFFFF;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:RIAN_archive_66514_Valentina_Nikolayeva-Tereshkova.jpg"><img alt="Tereshkova" data-file-height="1024" data-file-width="644" decoding="async" height="159" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/RIAN_archive_66514_Valentina_Nikolayeva-Tereshkova.jpg/100px-RIAN_archive_66514_Valentina_Nikolayeva-Tereshkova.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/RIAN_archive_66514_Valentina_Nikolayeva-Tereshkova.jpg/150px-RIAN_archive_66514_Valentina_Nikolayeva-Tereshkova.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/RIAN_archive_66514_Valentina_Nikolayeva-Tereshkova.jpg/200px-RIAN_archive_66514_Valentina_Nikolayeva-Tereshkova.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Valentina_Tereshkova" title="Valentina Tereshkova">Valentina Tereshkova</a></b>$<br/>(born 1937)<br/>cosmonaut, Hero of the Soviet Union, major general, politician\n</td>\n<td>Aboard <a href="/wiki/Vostok_6" title="Vostok 6">Vostok 6</a> on 16 June 1963 Tereshkova became the first woman as well as the first civilian to travel into space. On this mission, lasting almost three days in space, she performed various tests on herself to collect data on the reaction of the female body to spaceflight. She took photographs of the horizon, which were used to identify <a href="/wiki/Aerosol" title="Aerosol">aerosol</a> layers in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Earth_atmosphere" title="Earth atmosphere">Earth atmosphere</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133"><a href="#cite_note-133">[133]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tereshkova_crater" title="Tereshkova crater">Tereshkova crater</a> (Moon). <a href="/wiki/1671_Chaika" title="1671 Chaika">1671 Chaika</a> (minor planet, after Tereshkova\'s <a href="/wiki/Call_sign" title="Call sign">call sign</a>).</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Soviet_Union-1963-stamp-Valentina_Vladimirovna_Tereshkova.jpg"><img alt="Vostok 6 and Tereshkova" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="641" data-file-width="1280" decoding="async" height="60" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Soviet_Union-1963-stamp-Valentina_Vladimirovna_Tereshkova.jpg/120px-Soviet_Union-1963-stamp-Valentina_Vladimirovna_Tereshkova.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Soviet_Union-1963-stamp-Valentina_Vladimirovna_Tereshkova.jpg/180px-Soviet_Union-1963-stamp-Valentina_Vladimirovna_Tereshkova.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Soviet_Union-1963-stamp-Valentina_Vladimirovna_Tereshkova.jpg/240px-Soviet_Union-1963-stamp-Valentina_Vladimirovna_Tereshkova.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Soviet_Union-1963-stamp-Valentina_Vladimirovna_Tereshkova.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Vostok_6" title="Vostok 6">Vostok 6</a> and Tereshkova</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#fff8e7;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tillo_Alexej_Andreevitch.jpg"><img alt="Tillo" data-file-height="865" data-file-width="771" decoding="async" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Tillo_Alexej_Andreevitch.jpg/130px-Tillo_Alexej_Andreevitch.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Tillo_Alexej_Andreevitch.jpg/195px-Tillo_Alexej_Andreevitch.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Tillo_Alexej_Andreevitch.jpg/260px-Tillo_Alexej_Andreevitch.jpg 2x" width="130"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Aleksey_Tillo" title="Aleksey Tillo">Aleksey Tillo</a></b>~<br/>(1839&#8211;1900)<br/>geographer, cartographer, land surveyor, lieutenant general of the Russian Army\n</td>\n<td>Tillo created the first correct <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cartographic_relief_depiction" title="Cartographic relief depiction">relief map</a> of <a href="/wiki/European_Russia" title="European Russia">European Russia</a> in 1889. He coined the term <i><a href="/wiki/Central_Russian_Upland" title="Central Russian Upland">Central Russian Upland</a></i>. He measured the length of the main <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russian_rivers" title="Russian rivers">Russian rivers</a> and the level difference of the <a href="/wiki/Caspian_Sea" title="Caspian Sea">Caspian Sea</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sea_of_Aral" title="Sea of Aral">Sea of Aral</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134"><a href="#cite_note-134">[134]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Tillo_Islands" title="Tillo Islands">Tillo Islands</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lagekarte_Mittelrussische_Platte.png"><img alt="Central Russian Upland" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1664" data-file-width="2046" decoding="async" height="98" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Lagekarte_Mittelrussische_Platte.png/120px-Lagekarte_Mittelrussische_Platte.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Lagekarte_Mittelrussische_Platte.png/180px-Lagekarte_Mittelrussische_Platte.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Lagekarte_Mittelrussische_Platte.png/240px-Lagekarte_Mittelrussische_Platte.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Lagekarte_Mittelrussische_Platte.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Central_Russian_Upland" title="Central Russian Upland">Central Russian Upland</a> location</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#FFFFFF;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:RU072_10.jpg"><img alt="Titov" data-file-height="250" data-file-width="250" decoding="async" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/RU072_10.jpg/120px-RU072_10.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/RU072_10.jpg/180px-RU072_10.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/RU072_10.jpg/240px-RU072_10.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Gherman_Titov" title="Gherman Titov">Gherman Titov</a></b>$<br/>(1935&#8211;2000)<br/>cosmonaut, Hero of the Soviet Union\n</td>\n<td>Aboard <a href="/wiki/Vostok_2" title="Vostok 2">Vostok 2</a> on August 6, 1961, Titov became the second man to orbit the Earth, the first to do it multiple times (a total of 17), the first to spend more than a day in space, and the first person to drive a spaceship manually. He also was the first person to sleep in space and to suffer from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Space_sickness" title="Space sickness">space sickness</a>. He made the first manual photographs from orbit, thus setting a record for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Space_photography" title="Space photography">space photography</a>. A month short of 26 years old at launch, until this day he remains the youngest person to fly in space.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-135"><a href="#cite_note-135">[135]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Titov_(crater)" title="Titov (crater)">Titov (crater)</a> (Moon).</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center">\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#f0f8ff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Eduard_Toll.jpg"><img alt="Toll" data-file-height="388" data-file-width="270" decoding="async" height="144" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Eduard_Toll.jpg/100px-Eduard_Toll.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Eduard_Toll.jpg/150px-Eduard_Toll.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Eduard_Toll.jpg/200px-Eduard_Toll.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eduard_Toll" title="Eduard Toll">Eduard Toll</a></b><img alt="double-dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/>(1858&#8211;1902)<br/>zoologist, paleontologist, geologist\n</td>\n<td>In 1885&#8211;86, Baron Toll took part in an expedition to the <a href="/wiki/New_Siberian_Islands" title="New Siberian Islands">New Siberian Islands</a> led by <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Bunge" title="Alexander Bunge">Alexander Bunge</a>. In 1893 Toll led an academic expedition to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yakutia" title="Yakutia">Yakutia</a> and explored the region between the lower <a href="/wiki/Lena_River" title="Lena River">Lena</a> and <a href="/wiki/Khatanga_River" title="Khatanga River">Khatanga Rivers</a>, the basins of the <a href="/wiki/Yana_River" title="Yana River">Yana</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Indigirka" title="Indigirka">Indigirka</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kolyma_River" title="Kolyma River">Kolyma Rivers</a>, the plateau between the <a href="/wiki/Anabar_River" title="Anabar River">Anabar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Popigay_River" title="Popigay River">Popigay Rivers</a>, and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vasily_Pronchischev" title="Vasily Pronchischev">Vasily Pronchischev</a> mountain ridge (named by Toll) between the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Olenek_River" title="Olenek River">Olenek River</a> and the Anabar. In 1899, Toll took part in a voyage of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Icebreaker_Yermak" title="Icebreaker Yermak">icebreaker Yermak</a> to <a href="/wiki/Spitsbergen" title="Spitsbergen">Spitsbergen</a>, led by <a href="/wiki/Stepan_Makarov" title="Stepan Makarov">Stepan Makarov</a>. In 1900&#8211;02, Toll led an expedition on the ship <i><a href="/wiki/Zarya_(polar_ship)" title="Zarya (polar ship)">Zarya</a></i> to find the legendary <a href="/wiki/Sannikov_Land" title="Sannikov Land">Sannikov Land</a>. Due to severe ice conditions the expedition was forced to spend two winters in the <a href="/wiki/Arctic" title="Arctic">Arctic</a>. Toll traveled to <a href="/wiki/Bennett_Island" title="Bennett Island">Bennett Island</a> by sledge and kayak with three companions, and they were lost. In 1903 the search led by <a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Brusnev" title="Mikhail Brusnev">Mikhail Brusnev</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aleksandr_Kolchak" title="Aleksandr Kolchak">Aleksandr Kolchak</a> brought out the diaries and the collections of Toll\'s party.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Barr_64-2"><a href="#cite_note-Barr-64">[64]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Carte-Sakha.png"><img alt="Yakutia" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="876" data-file-width="834" decoding="async" height="126" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Carte-Sakha.png/120px-Carte-Sakha.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Carte-Sakha.png/180px-Carte-Sakha.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Carte-Sakha.png/240px-Carte-Sakha.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Carte-Sakha.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yakutia" title="Yakutia">Yakutia</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#ffdfff;">\n<th scope="row">\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Yevgeny_Tolstikov" title="Yevgeny Tolstikov">Yevgeny Tolstikov</a></b>&#167;<br/>(1913&#8211;1987)<br/>geographer, Hero of the Soviet Union\n</td>\n<td>In 1954 Tolstikov was the head of the <a href="/wiki/Drifting_ice_station" title="Drifting ice station">drifting ice station</a> North Pole-3 in the <a href="/wiki/Arctic" title="Arctic">Arctic</a>. In 1957&#8211;59 he led the <a href="/wiki/3rd_Soviet_Antarctic_Expedition" title="3rd Soviet Antarctic Expedition">3rd Soviet Antarctic Expedition</a> and founded the <a href="/wiki/Sovetskaya_(Antarctic_Research_Station)" title="Sovetskaya (Antarctic Research Station)">Sovetskaya</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pole_of_Inaccessibility_Antarctic_station" title="Pole of Inaccessibility Antarctic station">Pole of Inaccessibility Antarctic stations</a>. The expedition discovered the <a href="/wiki/Gamburtsev_Mountain_Range" title="Gamburtsev Mountain Range">Gamburtsev Mountain Range</a> and other features of <a href="/wiki/Antarctica" title="Antarctica">Antarctica</a> relief under the ice. Tolstikov was the chief editor of the general atlas of the <a href="/wiki/Antarctic" title="Antarctic">Antarctic</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136"><a href="#cite_note-136">[136]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/3357_Tolstikov" title="3357 Tolstikov">3357 Tolstikov</a> (minor planet).</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Southern_Pol_of_Inaccessibility_Henry_Cookson_team_n2i.JPG"><img alt="Pole of inaccessibility Antarctic station" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="916" data-file-width="1628" decoding="async" height="68" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Southern_Pol_of_Inaccessibility_Henry_Cookson_team_n2i.JPG/120px-Southern_Pol_of_Inaccessibility_Henry_Cookson_team_n2i.JPG" style="background:#dfdfff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Graf_f_tolstoy.jpg"><img alt="F.Tolstoy" data-file-height="485" data-file-width="366" decoding="async" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Graf_f_tolstoy.jpg/200px-Graf_f_tolstoy.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Fyodor_Ivanovich_Tolstoy" title="Fyodor Ivanovich Tolstoy">Fyodor Ivanovich Tolstoy</a></b>^<br/>(1782&#8211;1846)<br/>nobleman, adventurer\n</td>\n<td>A count from the <a href="/wiki/Tolstoy_family" title="Tolstoy family">Tolstoy family</a>, Fyodor Tolstoy was known for his unusual temper, gambling and passion for duels. In 1803 he took part in the <a href="/wiki/First_Russian_circumnavigation" title="First Russian circumnavigation">first Russian circumnavigation</a> on <a href="/wiki/Nadezhda_(1802_Russian_ship)" title="Nadezhda (1802 Russian ship)"><i>Nadezhda</i></a>, captained by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ivan_Krusenstern" title="Ivan Krusenstern">Ivan Krusenstern</a>. However, multiple quarrels with the crew and very bad behaviour, including successfully teaching a pet <a href="/wiki/Orangutan" title="Orangutan">orangutan</a> to cover the captain\'s longbook in ink, caused Tolstoy to be abandoned on a stop in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kamchatka" title="Kamchatka">Kamchatka</a> with the aforementioned ape, whose later fate is unknown. On a different ship Tolstoy managed to get into <a href="/wiki/Sitka,_Alaska" title="Sitka, Alaska">Sitka, Alaska</a>, where he spent several months among <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Alaskan_natives" title="Alaskan natives">Alaskan natives</a> of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tlingit_people" title="Tlingit people">Tlingit</a> tribe and acquired multiple tattoos. Finally he returned to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Petersburg" title="St. Petersburg">St. Petersburg</a> via Kamchatka and Siberia. His voyage to North America earned him the nickname <i>the American</i> and a legendary celebrity due to the tales and gossip of his adventures.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137"><a href="#cite_note-137">[137]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Tolstoy served as a prototype for a number of characters in Russian literature, including the duellist Zaretsky in <i><a href="/wiki/Eugene_Onegin" title="Eugene Onegin">Eugene Onegin</a></i> by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aleksandr_Pushkin" title="Aleksandr Pushkin">Aleksandr Pushkin</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pongo_pygmaeus_(orangutang).jpg"><img alt="An orangutan" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="771" decoding="async" height="156" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Pongo_pygmaeus_%28orangutang%29.jpg/100px-Pongo_pygmaeus_%28orangutang%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Pongo_pygmaeus_%28orangutang%29.jpg/150px-Pongo_pygmaeus_%28orangutang%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Pongo_pygmaeus_%28orangutang%29.jpg/200px-Pongo_pygmaeus_%28orangutang%29.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Pongo_pygmaeus_(orangutang).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>An <a href="/wiki/Orangutan" title="Orangutan">orangutan</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#ffdfff;">\n<th scope="row">\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Alexey_Tryoshnikov" title="Alexey Tryoshnikov">Alexey Tryoshnikov</a></b>&#167;<br/>(1914&#8211;1991)<br/>geographer, oceanologist\n</td>\n<td>Tryoshnikov participated in the 1948 Soviet expedition to the North Pole. In 1954&#8211;55, he headed the <a href="/wiki/Drifting_ice_station" title="Drifting ice station">drifting ice station</a> North Pole-3 in the <a href="/wiki/Arctic" title="Arctic">Arctic</a>. In 1956&#8211;58 he led the <a href="/wiki/2nd_Soviet_Antarctic_Expedition" title="2nd Soviet Antarctic Expedition">2nd</a> and in 1967&#8211;69 the <a href="/wiki/13th_Soviet_Antarctic_Expedition" title="13th Soviet Antarctic Expedition">13th Soviet Antarctic Expedition</a>, founding the <a href="/wiki/Bellingshausen_Station" title="Bellingshausen Station">Bellingshausen Station</a>. He took part in the creation of the general atlas of the <a href="/wiki/Antarctic" title="Antarctic">Antarctic</a> and was the main editor of the atlas of the Arctic. He was the president of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Soviet_Geographical_Society" title="Soviet Geographical Society">Soviet Geographical Society</a> in 1977&#8211;91 and the director of the <a href="/wiki/Arctic_and_Antarctic_Research_Institute" title="Arctic and Antarctic Research Institute">Arctic and Antarctic Research Institute</a> in 1960&#8211;81.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138"><a href="#cite_note-138">[138]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/3339_Treshnikov" title="3339 Treshnikov">3339 Treshnikov</a> (minor planet).</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" Tsivolko</a></b><img alt="double-dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/>(1810&#8211;1839)<br/>Russian Navy officer, hydrographer\n</td>\n<td>In 1832&#8211;34 Tsivolko made the first reliable maps of <a href="/wiki/Novaya_Zemlya" title="Novaya Zemlya">Novaya Zemlya</a>\'s southern shores together with <a href="/wiki/Pyotr_Pakhtusov" title="Pyotr Pakhtusov">Pyotr Pakhtusov</a>, and was the first to map the <a href="/wiki/Matochkin_Strait" title="Matochkin Strait">Matochkin Strait</a> between the two main islands of the archipelago. In 1837 he commanded the schooner <i>Krotov</i> during <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Karl_Baer" title="Karl Baer">Karl Baer</a>\'s expedition to Novaya Zemlya. In 1838 he died from scurvy while mapping the northern and northeastern shores of Novaya Zemlya.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139"><a href="#cite_note-139">[139]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:82px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Matochkin_Strait.svg"><img alt="Matochkin Strait" Zemlya">Novaya Zemlya</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#ffffd0;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Gombojab_Tsybikov" title="Gombojab Tsybikov">Gombojab Tsybikov</a></b>!<br/>(1873&#8211;1930)<br/>anthropologist, ethnographer, statesmen\n</td>\n<td>A native <a href="/wiki/Buryats" title="Buryats">Buryat</a>, Tsybikov traveled to <a href="/wiki/Tibet" title="Tibet">Tibet</a> in a group of Buryat and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kalmyk_people" title="Kalmyk people">Kalmyk</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Buddhist" title="Buddhist">Buddhist</a> pilgrims in 1899&#8211;1902. He became the first photographer of Tibet, taking pictures in secret. These pictures were widely celebrated throughout the world, printed by the <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Geographic_(magazine)" title="National Geographic (magazine)">National Geographic</a></i> in the U. S. In 1904 Tsybikov presented his pictures to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thubten_Gyatso,_13th_Dalai_Lama" title="Thubten Gyatso, 13th Dalai Lama">Dalai Lama</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ulan_Bator" title="Ulan Bator">Urga</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mongolia" title="Mongolia">Mongolia</a>. He published his travelogue with many valuable translations from <a href="/wiki/Standard_Tibetan" title="Standard Tibetan">Tibetan</a> included.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140"><a href="#cite_note-140">[140]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Potala-from-behind_07-2005.jpg"><img alt="Potala Palace, Tibet" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1920" data-file-width="2772" decoding="async" height="83" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/Potala-from-behind_07-2005.jpg/120px-Potala-from-behind_07-2005.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/Potala-from-behind_07-2005.jpg/180px-Potala-from-behind_07-2005.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/Potala-from-behind_07-2005.jpg/240px-Potala-from-behind_07-2005.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Potala-from-behind_07-2005.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Potala_Palace" title="Potala Palace">Potala Palace</a> in <a href="/wiki/Lhasa" title="Lhasa">Lhasa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tibet" title="Tibet">Tibet</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="U">U</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Russian_explorers&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: U">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div aria-labelledby="tocheading" class="toc plainlinks hlist" id="toc" role="navigation" style="text-align:left;">\n<div class="toctitle" id="toctitle" style="text-align:center;display:inline-block;"><span id="tocheading" style="font-weight:bold;">Contents:&#160;</span></div>\n<div style="margin:auto;white-space:nowrap;display:inline-block;">\n<ul><li><a href="#top">Top</a></li>\n<li><a href="#0&#8211;9">0&#8211;9</a></li>\n<li><a href="#A">A</a></li>\n<li><a href="#B">B</a></li>\n<li><a href="#C">C</a></li>\n<li><a href="#D">D</a></li>\n<li><a href="#E">E</a></li>\n<li><a href="#F">F</a></li>\n<li><a href="#G">G</a></li>\n<li><a href="#H">H</a></li>\n<li><a href="#I">I</a></li>\n<li><a href="#J">J</a></li>\n<li><a href="#K">K</a></li>\n<li><a href="#L">L</a></li>\n<li><a href="#M">M</a></li>\n<li><a href="#N">N</a></li>\n<li><a href="#O">O</a></li>\n<li><a href="#P">P</a></li>\n<li><a href="#Q">Q</a></li>\n<li><a href="#R">R</a></li>\n<li><a href="#S">S</a></li>\n<li><a href="#T">T</a></li>\n<li><a href="#U">U</a></li>\n<li><a href="#V">V</a></li>\n<li><a href="#W">W</a></li>\n<li><a href="#X">X</a></li>\n<li><a href="#Y">Y</a></li>\n<li><a href="#Z">Z</a> </li></ul>\n<p class="mw-empty-elt">\n</p>\n</div></div>\n<table class="wikitable">\n<tbody><tr style="background:#ccc;">\n<th scope="col" width="18%">Portrait\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="22%">Person\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="60%">Achievements\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Image\n</th></tr>\n<tr style="background:#dfdfff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Unkovskiy.jpg"><img alt="Unkovsky" data-file-height="800" data-file-width="608" decoding="async" height="132" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Unkovskiy.jpg/100px-Unkovskiy.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Unkovskiy.jpg/150px-Unkovskiy.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Unkovskiy.jpg/200px-Unkovskiy.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Ivan_Unkovsky" title="Ivan Unkovsky">Ivan Unkovsky</a></b>^<br/>(1822&#8211;1886)<br/>Russian admiral\n</td>\n<td>Unkovsky led an expedition on the frigate <i>Pallada</i>, together with Admiral <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yevfimy_Putyatin" title="Yevfimy Putyatin">Yevfimy Putyatin</a>, through the <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">Atlantic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Indian_Ocean" title="Indian Ocean">Indian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific Oceans</a> to Japan in 1852&#8211;55. This expedition contributed many important discoveries in <a href="/wiki/Oceanography" title="Oceanography">oceanography</a>. Described in the book by <a href="/wiki/Ivan_Goncharov" title="Ivan Goncharov">Ivan Goncharov</a>, who also sailed on the <i>Pallada</i>, it was a dangerous voyage since it coincided in time with the <a href="/wiki/Crimean_War" title="Crimean War">Crimean War</a> between Russia and the <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">Franco</a>-<a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> alliance. One of the results achieved was the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Shimoda" title="Treaty of Shimoda">Treaty of Shimoda</a> with Japan.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141"><a href="#cite_note-141">[141]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:FrigatePallada.jpg"><img alt="Frigate Pallada" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="647" data-file-width="900" decoding="async" height="86" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/FrigatePallada.jpg/120px-FrigatePallada.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/FrigatePallada.jpg/180px-FrigatePallada.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/FrigatePallada.jpg/240px-FrigatePallada.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:FrigatePallada.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Frigate <i><a href="/wiki/Athena" title="Athena">Pallada</a></i></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#f0f8ff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Urvantsev.jpg"><img alt="Urvantsev" data-file-height="580" data-file-width="400" decoding="async" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Urvantsev.jpg/100px-Urvantsev.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Urvantsev.jpg/150px-Urvantsev.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Urvantsev.jpg/200px-Urvantsev.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Nikolay_Urvantsev" title="Nikolay Urvantsev">Nikolay Urvantsev</a></b><img alt="double-dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/>(1893&#8211;1985)<br/>geologist\n</td>\n<td>Urvantsev was among the discoverers of a coal basin and a copper-nickel ore region in <a href="/wiki/Norilsk" title="Norilsk">Norilsk</a> in 1919&#8211;22 and was among the founders of Norilsk town. In 1922 he found evidence of the disappeared <a href="/wiki/Roald_Amundsen" title="Roald Amundsen">Roald Amundsen</a>\'s 1918 Arctic expedition crew members <a href="/wiki/Peter_Tessem_and_Paul_Knutsen" title="Peter Tessem and Paul Knutsen">Peter Tessem and Paul Knutsen</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Kara_Sea" title="Kara Sea">Kara Sea</a> shore. In 1930&#8211;32 Urvantsev and <a href="/wiki/Georgy_Ushakov" title="Georgy Ushakov">Georgy Ushakov</a> explored and completely mapped the <a href="/wiki/Severnaya_Zemlya" title="Severnaya Zemlya">Severnaya Zemlya</a> and established that it was an archipelago, discovering a number or major islands. Urvantsev also explored <a href="/wiki/Taymyr_Peninsula" title="Taymyr Peninsula">Taymyr Peninsula</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Central_Siberian_Plateau" title="Central Siberian Plateau">Central Siberian Plateau</a>. In 1933&#8211;34 aboard the <a href="/wiki/Steamer_Pravda" title="Steamer Pravda">Steamer Pravda</a> Urvantsev led the first Arctic <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Oil_exploration" title="Oil exploration">oil exploration</a> expedition.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bse_20-10"><a href="#cite_note-bse-20">[20]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Barr2_27-1"><a href="#cite_note-Barr2-27">[27]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Severnaya_Zemlya.svg"><img alt="Severnaya Zemlya" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="503" data-file-width="580" decoding="async" height="104" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Severnaya_Zemlya.svg/120px-Severnaya_Zemlya.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Severnaya_Zemlya.svg/180px-Severnaya_Zemlya.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Severnaya_Zemlya.svg/240px-Severnaya_Zemlya.svg.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Severnaya_Zemlya.svg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Severnaya_Zemlya" title="Severnaya Zemlya">Severnaya Zemlya</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#f0f8ff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Georgy_Ushakov.jpg"><img alt="Ushakov" data-file-height="245" data-file-width="170" decoding="async" height="144" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Georgy_Ushakov.jpg/100px-Georgy_Ushakov.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Georgy_Ushakov.jpg/150px-Georgy_Ushakov.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/fb/Georgy_Ushakov.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Georgy_Ushakov" title="Georgy Ushakov">Georgy Ushakov</a></b><img alt="double-dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/>(1901&#8211;1963)<br/>geographer\n</td>\n<td>In 1926 Ushakov founded the first Soviet settlement on <a href="/wiki/Wrangel_Island" title="Wrangel Island">Wrangel Island</a>. In 1930&#8211;32 Ushakov and <a href="/wiki/Nikolay_Urvantsev" title="Nikolay Urvantsev">Nikolay Urvantsev</a> explored and completely mapped the Severnaya Zemlya and established that it was an archipelago, the last one on Earth to be explored. In 1935&#8211;36 Ushakov led the first Soviet high-latitude expedition on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Icebreaker_Sadko" title="Icebreaker Sadko">icebreaker Sadko</a>, examining the last unexplored areas in the northern <a href="/wiki/Kara_Sea" title="Kara Sea">Kara Sea</a> and discovering <a href="/wiki/Ushakov_Island" title="Ushakov Island">Ushakov Island</a>, the last unknown island in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russian_Arctic" title="Russian Arctic">Russian Arctic</a> outside any archipelago. Ushakov died in Moscow, but was buried in Severnaya Zemlya.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ushakov_14-1"><a href="#cite_note-ushakov-14">[14]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Kara_seaUV.PNG"><img alt="Ushakov Island" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="534" data-file-width="710" decoding="async" height="90" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Kara_seaUV.PNG/120px-Kara_seaUV.PNG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Kara_seaUV.PNG/180px-Kara_seaUV.PNG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Kara_seaUV.PNG/240px-Kara_seaUV.PNG 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Kara_seaUV.PNG" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Ushakov_Island" title="Ushakov Island">Ushakov Island</a> location</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#dfffdf;">\n<th scope="row">\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Tatyana_Ustinova" title="Tatyana Ustinova">Tatyana Ustinova</a></b>*<br/>(1913&#8211;2009)<br/>geologist\n</td>\n<td>In 1940 Ustinova came to <a href="/wiki/Kronotsky_Nature_Reserve" title="Kronotsky Nature Reserve">Kronotsky Nature Reserve</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kamchatka" title="Kamchatka">Kamchatka</a>. In 1941, with the help of the local guide Anysyfor Krupenin, she discovered the <a href="/wiki/Valley_of_Geysers" title="Valley of Geysers">Valley of Geysers</a>, the second largest concentration of geysers in the world. She researched the geysers until 1946 and gave names to the most notable of them. She requested in a testament that her ashes were to be buried in the Valley of Geysers.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142"><a href="#cite_note-142">[142]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Valley_of_the_Geysers.jpg"><img alt="Valley of Geysers" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="768" data-file-width="1158" decoding="async" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Valley_of_the_Geysers.jpg/120px-Valley_of_the_Geysers.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Valley_of_the_Geysers.jpg/180px-Valley_of_the_Geysers.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Valley_of_the_Geysers.jpg/240px-Valley_of_the_Geysers.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Valley_of_the_Geysers.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Valley_of_Geysers" title="Valley of Geysers">Valley of Geysers</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kamchatka" title="Kamchatka">Kamchatka</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="V">V</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Russian_explorers&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: V">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div aria-labelledby="tocheading" class="toc plainlinks hlist" id="toc" role="navigation" style="text-align:left;">\n<div class="toctitle" id="toctitle" style="text-align:center;display:inline-block;"><span id="tocheading" style="font-weight:bold;">Contents:&#160;</span></div>\n<div style="margin:auto;white-space:nowrap;display:inline-block;">\n<ul><li><a href="#top">Top</a></li>\n<li><a href="#0&#8211;9">0&#8211;9</a></li>\n<li><a href="#A">A</a></li>\n<li><a href="#B">B</a></li>\n<li><a href="#C">C</a></li>\n<li><a href="#D">D</a></li>\n<li><a href="#E">E</a></li>\n<li><a href="#F">F</a></li>\n<li><a href="#G">G</a></li>\n<li><a </li></ul>\n<p class="mw-empty-elt">\n</p>\n</div></div>\n<table class="wikitable">\n<tbody><tr style="background:#ccc;">\n<th scope="col" width="18%">Portrait\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="22%">Person\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="60%">Achievements\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Image\n</th></tr>\n<tr style="background:#f0f8ff;">\n<th scope="row">\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Merkury_Vagin" title="Merkury Vagin">Merkury Vagin</a></b><img alt="double-dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/> (?&#8211;1712)<br/><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Siberian_Cossack" title="Siberian Cossack">Siberian Cossack</a>, seafarer, merchant\n</td>\n<td>In 1712, Vagin and his companion <a href="/wiki/Yakov_Permyakov" title="Yakov Permyakov">Yakov Permyakov</a> crossed the <a href="/wiki/Yana_Bay" title="Yana Bay">Yana Bay</a> over the ice and explored <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bolshoy_Lyakhovsky" title="Bolshoy Lyakhovsky">Bolshoy Lyakhovsky</a> island (sited two years earlier by Permyakov), spotting <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maly_Lyakhovsky" title="Maly Lyakhovsky">Maly Lyakhovsky</a> island from there. Thus they initiated the exploration of the large <a href="/wiki/New_Siberia" title="New Siberia">New Siberian</a> archipelago. On the way back they were murdered by mutineering expedition members.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143"><a href="#cite_note-143">[143]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:NewSiberianIslands.png"><img alt="New Siberia" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="178" data-file-width="300" decoding="async" height="71" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/NewSiberianIslands.png/120px-NewSiberianIslands.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/NewSiberianIslands.png/180px-NewSiberianIslands.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/NewSiberianIslands.png/240px-NewSiberianIslands.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:NewSiberianIslands.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/New_Siberian_Islands" title="New Siberian Islands">New Siberian Islands</a> location</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#ffe8d5;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Nikolai_Vavilov_NYWTS.jpg"><img alt="Vavilov" data-file-height="2593" data-file-width="1945" decoding="async" height="133" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Nikolai_Vavilov_NYWTS.jpg/100px-Nikolai_Vavilov_NYWTS.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Nikolai_Vavilov_NYWTS.jpg/150px-Nikolai_Vavilov_NYWTS.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Nikolai_Vavilov_NYWTS.jpg/200px-Nikolai_Vavilov_NYWTS.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Nikolai_Vavilov" title="Nikolai Vavilov">Nikolai Vavilov</a></b><img alt="dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/37/Dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/> (1887&#8211;1943)<br/>botanist and geneticist\n</td>\n<td>In 1924&#8211;35 Vavilov was the director of the <a href="/wiki/Institute_of_Plant_Industry" title="Institute of Plant Industry">Institute of Plant Industry</a>. He organized a series of botanical-agronomic expeditions, collected seeds from every corner of the globe, and created the world\'s largest collection of plant seeds in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Leningrad" title="Leningrad">Leningrad</a>. As a result of his explorations he identified the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vavilov_Center" title="Vavilov Center">centres of origin</a> of main cultivated plants.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144"><a href="#cite_note-144">[144]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vavilov_Institute_of_Plant_Industry" title="Vavilov Institute of Plant Industry">Vavilov Institute of Plant Industry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vavilovian_mimicry" title="Vavilovian mimicry">Vavilovian mimicry</a>; <a href="/wiki/2862_Vavilov" title="2862 Vavilov">2862 Vavilov</a> (minor planet), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vavilov_crater" title="Vavilov crater">Vavilov crater</a> (Moon) (named also after Vavilov\'s brother, physicist <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sergey_Vavilov" title="Sergey Vavilov">Sergey Vavilov</a>).</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Vavilov-center.jpg"><img alt="Vavilov Centers" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="614" data-file-width="1000" decoding="async" height="74" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Vavilov-center.jpg/120px-Vavilov-center.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Vavilov-center.jpg/180px-Vavilov-center.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Vavilov-center.jpg/240px-Vavilov-center.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Vavilov-center.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vavilov_Center" title="Vavilov Center">Vavilov Centers</a>: the origin of cultivated plants</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#f0f8ff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row">\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Boris_Vilkitsky" title="Boris Vilkitsky">Boris Vilkitsky</a></b><img alt="double-dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/>(1885&#8211;1961)<br/>Russian Navy captain, hydrographer\n</td>\n<td>In 1913&#8211;15 Vilkitsky led the <a href="/wiki/Arctic" title="Arctic">Arctic</a> hydrographic expedition on the icebreakers <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Icebreaker_Taymyr" title="Icebreaker Taymyr"><i>Taimyr</i></a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Icebreaker_Vaygach" title="Icebreaker Vaygach"><i>Vaigach</i></a>, exploring parts of the <a href="/wiki/Northern_Sea_Route" title="Northern Sea Route">Northern Sea Route</a>. In 1913, the expedition discovered <a href="/wiki/Severnaya_Zemlya" title="Severnaya Zemlya">Severnaya Zemlya</a>, the last archipelago on Earth to be explored. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vilkitsky_Island" title="Vilkitsky Island">Vilkitsky Island</a> was also discovered, as well as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maly_Taymyr" title="Maly Taymyr">Maly Taymyr</a> and <a href="/wiki/Starokadomsky_Island" title="Starokadomsky Island">Starokadomsky Islands</a>. In 1914&#8211;15, another Vilkitsky\'s expedition made the first through voyage from <a href="/wiki/Vladivostok" title="Vladivostok">Vladivostok</a> to <a href="/wiki/Arkhangelsk" title="Arkhangelsk">Arkhangelsk</a>, discovered <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zhokhova_Island" title="Zhokhova Island">Zhokhova Island</a> and described the southern coast of Severnaya Zemlya.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-vilkitsky_13-1"><a href="#cite_note-vilkitsky-13">[13]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Vilkitsky_Strait" title="Vilkitsky Strait">Vilkitsky Strait</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vilkitsky_Island_(Kara_Sea)" title="Vilkitsky Island (Kara Sea)">Vilkitsky Island (Kara Sea)</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vilkitsky_Island_(East_Siberian_Sea)" title="Vilkitsky Island (East Siberian Sea)">Vilkitsky Island (East Siberian Sea)</a></span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Kara_sea2SZ.PNG"><img alt="Severnaya Zemlya" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="534" data-file-width="701" decoding="async" height="91" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/Kara_sea2SZ.PNG/120px-Kara_sea2SZ.PNG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/Kara_sea2SZ.PNG/180px-Kara_sea2SZ.PNG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/Kara_sea2SZ.PNG/240px-Kara_sea2SZ.PNG 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Kara_sea2SZ.PNG" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Severnaya_Zemlya" title="Severnaya Zemlya">Severnaya Zemlya</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#f0f8ff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row">\n</th>\n<td><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vladimir_Vize" title="Vladimir Vize">Vladimir Vize</a></b><img alt="double-dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/>(1886&#8211;1954)<br/>oceanographer\n</td>\n<td>In 1912&#8211;14 Vize took part in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Georgiy_Sedov" title="Georgiy Sedov">Georgiy Sedov</a>\'s expedition to <a href="/wiki/Novaya_Zemlya" title="Novaya Zemlya">Novaya Zemlya</a> and <a href="/wiki/Franz_Josef_Land" title="Franz Josef Land">Franz Josef Land</a>. In 1924 he studied the drift of <a href="/wiki/Georgy_Brusilov" title="Georgy Brusilov">Georgy Brusilov</a>\'s ill-fated ship <a href="/wiki/Svyataya_Anna" title="Svyataya Anna"><i>St. Anna</i></a>, trapped on pack ice. As a result of this study he predicted the location of the yet unseen <a href="/wiki/Vize_Island" title="Vize Island">Vize Island</a>, based on the analysis of ice movement in the <a href="/wiki/Kara_Sea" title="Kara Sea">Kara Sea</a>. He took part in the first successful crossing of the Northern Sea Route in a single navigation on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Icebreaker_Sibiryakov" title="Icebreaker Sibiryakov">icebreaker Sibiryakov</a> in 1932. In 1938&#8211;40 he conducted scientific research on the ice-captured <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Icebreaker_Sedov" title="Icebreaker Sedov">icebreaker Sedov</a>, turned into a <a href="/wiki/Drifting_ice_station" title="Drifting ice station">drifting ice station</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bse_20-11"><a href="#cite_note-bse-20">[20]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Vize_Island" title="Vize Island">Vize Island</a></span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Kara_seaVZ.PNG"><img alt="Vize Island" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="534" data-file-width="710" decoding="async" height="90" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Kara_seaVZ.PNG/120px-Kara_seaVZ.PNG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Kara_seaVZ.PNG/180px-Kara_seaVZ.PNG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Kara_seaVZ.PNG/240px-Kara_seaVZ.PNG 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Kara_seaVZ.PNG" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Vize_Island" title="Vize Island">Vize Island</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Kara_Sea" title="Kara Sea">Kara Sea</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#f0f8ff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row">\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Voronin_(captain)" title="Vladimir Voronin (captain)">Vladimir Voronin</a></b><img alt="double-dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/> (1890&#8211;1952)<br/>Soviet Navy captain\n</td>\n<td>In 1932 Voronin commanded the expedition of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Icebreaker_Sibiryakov" title="Icebreaker Sibiryakov">icebreaker Sibiryakov</a> which made the first successful crossing of the <a href="/wiki/Northern_Sea_Route" title="Northern Sea Route">Northern Sea Route</a> in a single navigation without wintering, in 65 days from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Archangelsk" title="Archangelsk">Archangelsk</a> to <a href="/wiki/Yokohama" title="Yokohama">Yokohama</a> in Japan. In 1933&#8211;34 he commanded the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chelyuskin_steamship" title="Chelyuskin steamship">Chelyuskin steamship</a> with the scientific expedition of <a href="/wiki/Otto_Schmidt" title="Otto Schmidt">Otto Schmidt</a> aboard. The ship became ice-bound in the <a href="/wiki/Chukchi_Sea" title="Chukchi Sea">Chukchi Sea</a>, but almost all the crew was resqued by planes from their camp on the ice.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-145"><a href="#cite_note-145">[145]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Voronina_Island" title="Voronina Island">Voronina Island</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:A_Sibirykov.jpg"><img alt="Icebreaker Sibiryakov" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="466" data-file-width="674" decoding="async" height="83" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/A_Sibirykov.jpg/120px-A_Sibirykov.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/A_Sibirykov.jpg/180px-A_Sibirykov.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/A_Sibirykov.jpg/240px-A_Sibirykov.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:A_Sibirykov.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Icebreaker_Sibiryakov" title="Icebreaker Sibiryakov">Icebreaker Sibiryakov</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="W">W</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Russian_explorers&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: W">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div aria-labelledby="tocheading" class="toc plainlinks hlist" id="toc" role="navigation" style="text-align:left;">\n<div class="toctitle" id="toctitle" style="text-align:center;display:inline-block;"><span id="tocheading" style="font-weight:bold;">Contents:&#160;</span></div>\n<div style="margin:auto;white-space:nowrap;display:inline-block;">\n<ul><li><a href="#top">Top</a></li>\n<li><a href="#0&#8211;9">0&#8211;9</a></li>\n<li><a href="#A">A</a></li>\n<li><a </li></ul>\n<p class="mw-empty-elt">\n</p>\n</div></div>\n<table class="wikitable">\n<tbody><tr style="background:#ccc;">\n<th scope="col" width="18%">Portrait\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="22%">Person\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="60%">Achievements\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Image\n</th></tr>\n<tr style="background:#f0f8ff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%D0%92%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B3%D0%B5%D0%BB%D1%8C_%D0%A4%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4_%D0%9F%D0%B5%D1%82%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87.jpg"><img alt="Wrangel" data-file-height="1484" data-file-width="1201" decoding="async" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/%D0%92%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B3%D0%B5%D0%BB%D1%8C_%D0%A4%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4_%D0%9F%D0%B5%D1%82%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87.jpg/100px-%D0%92%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B3%D0%B5%D0%BB%D1%8C_%D0%A4%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4_%D0%9F%D0%B5%D1%82%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/%D0%92%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B3%D0%B5%D0%BB%D1%8C_%D0%A4%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4_%D0%9F%D0%B5%D1%82%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87.jpg/150px-%D0%92%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B3%D0%B5%D0%BB%D1%8C_%D0%A4%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4_%D0%9F%D0%B5%D1%82%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8e/%D0%92%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B3%D0%B5%D0%BB%D1%8C_%D0%A4%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4_%D0%9F%D0%B5%D1%82%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87.jpg/200px-%D0%92%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B3%D0%B5%D0%BB%D1%8C_%D0%A4%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4_%D0%9F%D0%B5%D1%82%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Ferdinand_von_Wrangel" title="Ferdinand von Wrangel">Ferdinand von Wrangel</a></b><img alt="double-dagger" data-file-height="14" data-file-width="9" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" width="9"/><br/> (1797&#8211;1870)<br/>Russian admiral, colonial administrator\n</td>\n<td>Ferdinand Wrangel took part in <a href="/wiki/Vasily_Golovnin" title="Vasily Golovnin">Vasily Golovnin</a>\'s world cruise on the ship <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kamchatka" title="Kamchatka">Kamchatka</a></i> in 1817&#8211;19. In 1820&#8211;24 Wrangel sailed north of the <a href="/wiki/Kolyma_River" title="Kolyma River">Kolyma River</a> and established that there was an open sea, not dry land, as was previously thought. Together with <a href="/wiki/Fyodor_Matyushkin" title="Fyodor Matyushkin">Fyodor Matyushkin</a> and P. Kuzmin, he described the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Medvyezhi_Islands" title="Medvyezhi Islands">Medvyezhi Islands</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Arctic" title="Arctic">Arctic</a> coastline from the <a href="/wiki/Indigirka_River" title="Indigirka River">Indigirka River</a> to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kolyuchinskaya_Bay" title="Kolyuchinskaya Bay">Kolyuchinskaya Bay</a>. After noticing swarms of birds flying north and questioning the native population, he determined that there must be an undiscovered island in the <a href="/wiki/Arctic_Ocean" title="Arctic Ocean">Arctic Ocean</a>. Even though his search for it was unsuccessful the island was later named <a href="/wiki/Wrangel_Island" title="Wrangel Island">Wrangel Island</a>. Wrangel led the circumnavigation on the ship <i>Krotky</i> in 1825&#8211;27. He was the governor of <a href="/wiki/Russian_America" title="Russian America">Russian America</a> in 1829&#8211;35, the president of the <a href="/wiki/Russian-American_Company" title="Russian-American Company">Russian-American Company</a> in 1840&#8211;49 and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Heads_of_military_of_Imperial_Russia#Ministry_of_Sea_Forces" title="Heads of military of Imperial Russia">Minister of the Navy</a> in 1855&#8211;57. In 1845 he became one of the founders of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russian_Geographic_Society" title="Russian Geographic Society">Russian Geographic Society</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146"><a href="#cite_note-146">[146]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a href="/wiki/Wrangel_Island" title="Wrangel Island">Wrangel Island</a> (<a href="/wiki/Chukchi_Sea" title="Chukchi Sea">Chukchi Sea</a>), <a href="/wiki/Wrangell_Island" title="Wrangell Island">Wrangell Island</a> in <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Archipelago" title="Alexander Archipelago">Alexander Archipelago</a>; <a href="/wiki/Wrangell,_Alaska" title="Wrangell, Alaska">Wrangell, Alaska</a>; <a href="/wiki/Wrangell_Narrows" title="Wrangell Narrows">Wrangell Narrows</a> <a href="/wiki/Cape_Wrangell" title="Cape Wrangell">Cape Wrangell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mount_Wrangell" title="Mount Wrangell">Mount Wrangell</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Medvyezhi_map.png"><img alt="Medvyezhi Islands" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Medvyezhi_map.png/180px-Medvyezhi_map.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Medvyezhi_map.png/240px-Medvyezhi_map.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Medvyezhi_map.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Medvyezhi_Islands" title="Medvyezhi Islands">Medvyezhi Islands</a> location</div></div></div></div><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Siberia_WR.png"><img alt="Wrangel Island" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="409" data-file-width="710" decoding="async" height="69" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Siberia_WR.png/120px-Siberia_WR.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Siberia_WR.png/180px-Siberia_WR.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Siberia_WR.png/240px-Siberia_WR.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Siberia_WR.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Wrangel_Island" title="Wrangel Island">Wrangel Island</a> in the Arctic</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Y">Y</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Russian_explorers&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Y">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div aria-labelledby="tocheading" class="toc plainlinks hlist" id="toc" role="navigation" style="text-align:left;">\n<div class="toctitle" id="toctitle" style="text-align:center;display:inline-block;"><span id="tocheading" style="font-weight:bold;">Contents:&#160;</span></div>\n<div style="margin:auto;white-space:nowrap;display:inline-block;">\n<ul><li><a href="#top">Top</a></li>\n<li><a href="#0&#8211;9">0&#8211;9</a></li>\n<li><a href="#A">A</a></li>\n<li><a href="#B">B</a></li>\n<li><a href="#C">C</a></li>\n<li><a href="#D">D</a></li>\n<li><a href="#E">E</a></li>\n<li><a href="#F">F</a></li>\n<li><a href="#G">G</a></li>\n<li><a href="#N">N</a></li>\n<li><a href="#O">O</a></li>\n<li><a href="#P">P</a></li>\n<li><a href="#Q">Q</a></li>\n<li><a href="#R">R</a></li>\n<li><a href="#S">S</a></li>\n<li><a </li></ul>\n<p class="mw-empty-elt">\n</p>\n</div></div>\n<table class="wikitable">\n<tbody><tr style="background:#ccc;">\n<th scope="col" width="18%">Portrait\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="22%">Person\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="60%">Achievements\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Image\n</th></tr>\n<tr style="background:#ffffd0;">\n<th align="center" scope="row">\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Nikolai_Yadrintsev" title="Nikolai Yadrintsev">Nikolai Yadrintsev</a></b>!<br/>(1842&#8211;1894)<br/>public figure, archaeologist, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turkologist" title="Turkologist">turkologist</a>\n</td>\n<td>In 1889 Yadrintsev located the remains of the medieval city Hara-Balgas and <a href="/wiki/Genghis_Khan" title="Genghis Khan">Genghis Khan</a>\'s capital <a href="/wiki/Karakorum" title="Karakorum">Karakorum</a> in <a href="/wiki/Mongolia" title="Mongolia">Mongolia</a>. In the valley of the <a href="/wiki/Orkhon_River" title="Orkhon River">Orkhon River</a> he discovered the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Orkhon_script" title="Orkhon script">Orkhon script</a> of the ancient <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/T%C3%BCrks" title="T&#252;rks">T&#252;rks</a> on two petroglyphic monuments with runiform writing, later decoded by the Danish scientist <a href="/wiki/Vilhelm_Thomsen" title="Vilhelm Thomsen">Vilhelm Thomsen</a>. In 1891 Yadrintsev together with <a href="/wiki/Vasily_Radlov" title="Vasily Radlov">Vasily Radlov</a> found more monuments of T&#252;rkic runiform writing.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147"><a href="#cite_note-147">[147]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Karakorum_-_Tortue_Sud.jpg"><img alt="A stone turtle in Karakorum" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="375" data-file-width="500" decoding="async" height="90" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Karakorum_-_Tortue_Sud.jpg/120px-Karakorum_-_Tortue_Sud.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Karakorum_-_Tortue_Sud.jpg/180px-Karakorum_-_Tortue_Sud.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Karakorum_-_Tortue_Sud.jpg/240px-Karakorum_-_Tortue_Sud.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Karakorum_-_Tortue_Sud.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A stone turtle in <a href="/wiki/Karakorum" title="Karakorum">Karakorum</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mongolia" title="Mongolia">Mongolia</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#dfffdf;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Yermak_Timofeyevich.jpg"><img alt="Yermak" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="346" decoding="async" height="139" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Yermak_Timofeyevich.jpg/100px-Yermak_Timofeyevich.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Yermak_Timofeyevich.jpg/150px-Yermak_Timofeyevich.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Yermak_Timofeyevich.jpg/200px-Yermak_Timofeyevich.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Yermak_Timofeyevich" title="Yermak Timofeyevich">Yermak Timofeyevich</a></b>*<br/> (1532/42&#8211;1585)<br/>Cossack ataman, folk hero\n</td>\n<td>Around 1577, the merchants <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Stroganovs" title="Stroganovs">Stroganovs</a>, who were the main colonisers of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Urals" title="Urals">Urals</a>, hired Yermak to protect their lands from attacks by the Siberian <a href="/wiki/Khan_(title)" title="Khan (title)">Khan</a> <a href="/wiki/Kuchum" title="Kuchum">Kuchum</a>. The Russians planned to attack Kuchum in his own land, and in 1581 Yermak penetrated into Siberia. After a few victories over the khan\'s army, Yermak\'s Cossacks defeated Kuchum\'s main forces on the <a href="/wiki/Irtysh_River" title="Irtysh River">Irtysh River</a> in a 3-day <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Chuvash_Cape" title="Battle of Chuvash Cape">Battle of Chuvash Cape</a> in 1582, forcing them to retreat to the steppes. Thus Yermak <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Conquest_of_the_Khanate_of_Siberia" title="Conquest of the Khanate of Siberia">captured</a> the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Siberia_Khanate" title="Siberia Khanate">Siberia Khanate</a>, including its capital <a href="/wiki/Qashliq" title="Qashliq">Qashliq</a> near modern <a href="/wiki/Tobolsk" title="Tobolsk">Tobolsk</a>. Kuchum was still strong and suddenly attacked Yermak in 1585 in the dead of night, killing most of his people. Yermak was wounded and tried to swim across the Wagay River (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Irtysh" title="Irtysh">Irtysh</a>\'s tributary), but drowned under the weight of his own <a href="/wiki/Chain_mail" title="Chain mail">chain mail</a> armor. The Cossacks had to withdraw from Siberia completely, but thanks to Yermak\'s having explored the main river routes of <a href="/wiki/West_Siberian_Plain" title="West Siberian Plain">West Siberian Plain</a>, the Russians successfully recaptured all Yermak\'s conquests just a few years later.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-yermak_5-1"><a href="#cite_note-yermak-5">[5]</a></sup><br/><br/><span style="font-size:85%;">Named in honor: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Icebreaker_Yermak" title="Icebreaker Yermak">Icebreaker Yermak</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yermak_Stone" title="Yermak Stone">Yermak Stone</a>.</span>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:YermakLubok.jpg"><img alt="Yermak on a lubok print" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="478" data-file-width="611" decoding="async" height="94" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/YermakLubok.jpg/120px-YermakLubok.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/YermakLubok.jpg/180px-YermakLubok.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/YermakLubok.jpg/240px-YermakLubok.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:YermakLubok.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i>Yermak Timofeyevich the Conqueror of Siberia</i>, <a href="/wiki/Lubok" title="Lubok">lubok</a></div></div></div></div><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ob_watershed.png"><img alt="Ob\'-Irtysh basin" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="988" data-file-width="988" decoding="async" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/Ob_watershed.png/120px-Ob_watershed.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/Ob_watershed.png/180px-Ob_watershed.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/Ob_watershed.png/240px-Ob_watershed.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Ob_watershed.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ob%27" title="Ob\'">Ob\'</a>-<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Irtysh" title="Irtysh">Irtysh</a> basin</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Z">Z</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Russian_explorers&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Z">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div aria-labelledby="tocheading" class="toc plainlinks hlist" id="toc" role="navigation" style="text-align:left;">\n<div class="toctitle" id="toctitle" style="text-align:center;display:inline-block;"><span id="tocheading" style="font-weight:bold;">Contents:&#160;</span></div>\n<div style="margin:auto;white-space:nowrap;display:inline-block;">\n<ul><li><a href="#top">Top</a></li>\n<li><a href="#0&#8211;9">0&#8211;9</a></li>\n<li><a href="#A">A</a></li>\n<li><a href="#B">B</a></li>\n<li><a href="#C">C</a></li>\n<li><a href="#D">D</a></li>\n<li><a href="#E">E</a></li>\n<li><a href="#F">F</a></li>\n<li><a href="#G">G</a></li>\n<li><a href="#H">H</a></li>\n<li><a href="#I">I</a></li>\n<li><a href="#J">J</a></li>\n<li><a href="#K">K</a></li>\n<li><a href="#L">L</a></li>\n<li><a href="#M">M</a></li>\n<li><a href="#N">N</a></li>\n<li><a href="#O">O</a></li>\n<li><a href="#P">P</a></li>\n<li><a href="#Q">Q</a></li>\n<li><a href="#R">R</a></li>\n<li><a href="#S">S</a></li>\n<li><a </li></ul>\n<p class="mw-empty-elt">\n</p>\n</div></div>\n<table class="wikitable">\n<tbody><tr style="background:#ccc;">\n<th scope="col" width="18%">Portrait\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="22%">Person\n</th>\n<th scope="col" width="60%">Achievements\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Image\n</th></tr>\n<tr style="background:#dfdfff;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lavrenty_Zagoskin.jpg"><img alt="Zagoskin" data-file-height="192" data-file-width="146" decoding="async" height="132" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Lavrenty_Zagoskin.jpg/100px-Lavrenty_Zagoskin.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/d/d1/Lavrenty_Zagoskin.jpg 1.5x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Lavrenty_Zagoskin" title="Lavrenty Zagoskin">Lavrenty Zagoskin</a></b>^<br/>(1808&#8211;1890)<br/>Russian Navy officer, naturalist\n</td>\n<td>Commissioned by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russian_America_Company" title="Russian America Company">Russian America Company</a>, in 1842&#8211;44 Zagoskin traveled extensively in Alaska, covering more than 3300&#160;miles. He explored and mapped the <a href="/wiki/Yukon_River" title="Yukon River">Yukon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kuskokwim_River" title="Kuskokwim River">Kuskokwim</a>, <a href="/wiki/Innoko_River" title="Innoko River">Innoko</a> and <a href="/wiki/Koyukuk_River" title="Koyukuk River">Koyukuk Rivers</a>, and researched the native peoples and nature of the region. He published the first detailed description of the inner areas of <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148"><a href="#cite_note-148">[148]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Yukon_watershed.png"><img alt="Yukon basin" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="500" decoding="async" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Yukon_watershed.png/120px-Yukon_watershed.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Yukon_watershed.png/180px-Yukon_watershed.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Yukon_watershed.png/240px-Yukon_watershed.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Yukon_watershed.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Yukon_River" title="Yukon River">Yukon River</a> basin</div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr>\n<tr style="background:#dfffdf;">\n<th align="center" scope="row"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%A1%D1%82%D0%B5%D0%BF%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87_%D0%97%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%BE%D0%B9%D0%BA%D0%BE.jpg"><img alt="Zavoyko" data-file-height="766" data-file-width="580" decoding="async" height="132" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%A1%D1%82%D0%B5%D0%BF%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87_%D0%97%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%BE%D0%B9%D0%BA%D0%BE.jpg/100px-%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%A1%D1%82%D0%B5%D0%BF%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87_%D0%97%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%BE%D0%B9%D0%BA%D0%BE.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%A1%D1%82%D0%B5%D0%BF%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87_%D0%97%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%BE%D0%B9%D0%BA%D0%BE.jpg/150px-%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%A1%D1%82%D0%B5%D0%BF%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87_%D0%97%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%BE%D0%B9%D0%BA%D0%BE.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%A1%D1%82%D0%B5%D0%BF%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87_%D0%97%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%BE%D0%B9%D0%BA%D0%BE.jpg/200px-%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%A1%D1%82%D0%B5%D0%BF%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87_%D0%97%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%BE%D0%B9%D0%BA%D0%BE.jpg 2x" width="100"/></a>\n</th>\n<td><b><a href="/wiki/Vasily_Zavoyko" title="Vasily Zavoyko">Vasily Zavoyko</a></b>*<br/> (1809&#8211;1898)<br/>Russian admiral\n</td>\n<td>In 1835&#8211;38 Zavoyko twice circumnavigated the globe. After 1840, during his service for the Russian-American Company in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Okhotsk_Sea" title="Okhotsk Sea">Okhotsk Sea</a>, Zavoyko explored the estuary of the <a href="/wiki/Amur_River" title="Amur River">Amur River</a>. His reports led to further expeditions and ultimately the incorporation of <a href="/wiki/Primorsky_Krai" title="Primorsky Krai">Primorsky Krai</a> into Russia. In 1854, at the time of <a href="/wiki/Crimean_War" title="Crimean War">Crimean War</a>, Zavoyko led the successful defence of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kamchatka" title="Kamchatka">Kamchatka</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Siege_of_Petropavlovsk" title="Siege of Petropavlovsk">Siege of Petropavlovsk</a>. He repelled the superior allied British-French forces and even captured the <a href="/wiki/Union_Jack" title="Union Jack">Union Jack</a>. In 1855, making his way through the frozen seas and successfully avoiding the large enemy fleet, he supervised the transfer of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russian_Pacific_Fleet" title="Russian Pacific Fleet">Russian Pacific Fleet</a> from Petropavlovsk to <a href="/wiki/Nikolayevsk-on-Amur" title="Nikolayevsk-on-Amur">Nikolayevsk-on-Amur</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Petropavlovsk_center_port.jpg"><img alt="Petropavlovsk-Kamchatsky" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="519" data-file-width="777" decoding="async" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Petropavlovsk_center_port.jpg/120px-Petropavlovsk_center_port.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Petropavlovsk_center_port.jpg/180px-Petropavlovsk_center_port.jpg 1.5x, class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Petropavlovsk_center_port.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Petropavlovsk-Kamchatsky" title="Petropavlovsk-Kamchatsky">Petropavlovsk-Kamchatsky</a></div></div></div></div>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span
